The [Manchukuo] authorities also lodged a verbal protest regarding this case. The officials in Harbin believe that the time for negotiation has passed and that retaliatory action should be taken. (Dispatch from Reuters on the 10th)

Geneva Disarmament Conference Approaching Reopening

Japan Decides on Response Strategy 30

(Tokyo) According to a report from Ambassador Satō to Belgium, the general disarmament conference in Geneva is scheduled to reopen its working committee on the 6th of next month to report on Henderson's discussions with representatives from the United States, France, Italy, and Germany during his summer visit regarding British proposals. Regarding the army, it is proposed to limit tanks and poison gas. As for the naval issue, the status quo will be maintained, pending detailed discussions at the Washington and London conferences. The conference will make a formal resolution on these matters and convene a general committee on October 17 to continue discussing the aforementioned formal resolution. The Japanese government has decided to send Ambassador Satō Naotake to Belgium, Ambassador Mushanokōji Kintomo to Germany, and Vice Admiral Hase Shūshin as representatives to attend the conference. As a result of Satō's negotiations with Henderson during the summer break, it is known that the representatives of the major participating countries have a considerable understanding of Henderson's proposals (except for the issue of military strength). However, the Japanese government, citing the fact that the London Treaty only has provisional effect, has instructed Ambassador Satō to oppose the idea of maintaining the status quo. Regarding the issue of limiting naval forces, it advocates for the abolition of aircraft carriers and submarines and the prohibition of aerial bombing. Although the current conference will not conclude a numerical limitation agreement on the nature and quantity of armaments, but will only decide on an abstract formal resolution, the Japanese representatives plan to continue to adhere to the established policy and advocate for Japan's proposals, so a fierce and arduous battle will be inevitable. (Dispatch from the Japanese United Press on the 10th)

Japan Plans to Establish a Ten-Year Diplomatic Plan for China

Will be Based on the Legacy of Komura Jutarō 31

Changing the Previous Policy of Ad Hoc Improvisation

Various Departments Ordered to Engage in Preparatory Work

The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun published on the 5th that Foreign Minister Uchida, in order to restore the Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations, which are currently in a state of flux, to normalcy, has decided, after six months of observing a policy of wait-and-see, to conduct direct negotiations with China at the end of this year (late November or early December). Regarding the specific strategies for direct negotiations, important instructions will be sent to Ambassador to China Ariyoshi Akira. Recently, he has also separately and strictly ordered Vice Minister Shigemitsu, Director of the Asia Bureau Kuwajima, and the three section chiefs of the Asia Bureau to engage in preparatory work regarding the establishment of a new policy toward China. The reason why the start of negotiations is scheduled for after the end of November is that the outline of China's policy toward Japan must be realized after the resolutions of the Third Lushan Conference and the Fifth Plenary Session, which requires at least two more months. At that time, the Japanese side will adopt a policy of peace or war depending on the attitude of the Chinese side. Furthermore, the main objective of the new China policy that Foreign Minister Uchida cherishes is to change the previous conciliatory policy of ad hoc improvisation and to establish a permanent and effective (at least ten-year) basic principle, which can be called a ten-year diplomatic plan for China. This principle will be based on the legacy of the late Marquis Komura Jutarō's [positive policy toward China]. Currently, Foreign Minister Uchida has ordered the aforementioned heads of relevant departments to investigate Sino-Japanese commercial trade relations, investment status, railways, transportation matters such as shipping, and Japanese cultural facilities in China, and to prepare a report as soon as possible, which is expected to be completed by the end of this year. Also, when direct negotiations begin, the preconditions that the Japanese side will propose are: (1) Thorough suppression of anti-Japanese and anti-Japanese goods movements throughout China; (2) Cessation of treaty and contract violations; (3) Confirmation of whether there is an intention to form a Sino-Japanese economic alliance.) (World News Agency)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Foreign Ministry is planning a ten-year diplomatic plan for China, in which the plan for North China is to complete new loans for the three major railways. The so-called three major railways in the minds of the Japanese are: (1) Connection of the Longhai Railway and the Shandong Railway; (2) Renovation of the Beijing-Suiyuan Railway; (3) Construction rights for the Jinzhang Railway (from Jinzhou via Chengde to Zhangjiakou). It is said that a certain diplomat who is the main culprit of the Twenty-One Demands, under the instructions of the Japanese, is actively lobbying. (Dispatch from the China United Press on the 10th)

Japan Consolidates its Military Strength

Major Reform to be Implemented in the Army System 32

(Tokyo) Since the Shanghai War, the Japanese army has deeply felt that relying solely on the Yamato spirit cannot guarantee victory on the battlefield. The bravery shown by the 19th Route Army proves that the Chinese spirit cannot be taken lightly. Therefore, reforming military equipment and supplementing firepower, even when fighting against China, will be very difficult after our air force is complete. It is said that the Japanese military has ordered the expeditionary force, the Technical Headquarters, the Army Scientific Research Institute, the Fortification Headquarters, the Aviation Headquarters, the Clothing Factory, the Food Factory, the schools of various arms, and the General Staff Headquarters, etc., to form a committee to study reform matters. It is scheduled to complete the improvement of its military equipment by 1938, that is, to add some modifications to the original plan drafted by the military system investigation committee in June 1931 and implement it. The content of the so-called original plan of the Military Investigation Committee is as follows:

Enhancing Combat Power 33

(1) Increase the number of heavy machine guns for infantry in unit formations. According to the Japanese, each division previously focused on light machine guns, with each division equipped with 300 light machine guns and 50 heavy machine guns. This will be changed to a policy of parallel light and heavy machine guns. (2) Abolish old-fashioned infantry cannons and replace them with new-style infantry cannons with stronger firepower to increase combat power. (3) Cavalry regiments must be equipped with a sufficient number of heavy machine guns and armored vehicles. (4) Increase the number of light howitzers assigned to the artillery of each division to increase artillery attack power.

Increasing Troops Stationed in Manchuria 34

Before the September 18th Incident, the Japanese troops stationed in the Three Eastern Provinces consisted of one division of the Kwantung Army and six battalions of the Independent Garrison. The Japanese General Staff Headquarters had planned to transfer five divisions to Manchuria before the incident, but it was opposed by Foreign Minister Shidehara on the grounds of violating treaties, which prevented it from being realized. The Japanese military then created a new situation by force, allowing it to create a pseudo-state, allowing the Japanese to increase troops at will. The funds required for this plan will be decided by the 65th National Diet.

Increasing Troops in Taiwan and Korea 35

The troops stationed in Korea originally consisted of two divisions and an independent garrison. It is planned to increase one division to three divisions and one independent garrison to deal with Soviet Russia. Taiwan, due to its rugged terrain and difficulty in combat, and burdened with the mission of fighting in South China, needs to add an engineer battalion. This plan was realized in 1932.

Expansion of the Air Force 36

In modern land and sea warfare, the air force is the criterion for determining victory or defeat. Therefore, air squadrons, anti-aircraft artillery squadrons, and air observation squadrons should be added. The Japanese Navy has decided to increase eight squadrons starting from next spring, and the Army will also increase the number of aircraft by one time. The personnel have been increasing by 100 people per term since 1932.

Mechanization of the Military 37

Russia has four mechanized army groups with five hundred tanks. Japan also wants to increase this type of military equipment, with the aim of being on par with Russia. According to Japan's own claim, Japan only has forty tanks.

Research on Chemical Warfare 38

In future land warfare, poison gas warfare is inevitable. Therefore, specialized schools should be established to study the manufacturing of poison gas weapons and anti-gas measures, and to train in poison gas warfare and anti-gas work.

Training Junior Officers 39

In modern warfare, the command and control capabilities of non-commissioned officers are one of the main conditions for victory. The existing training institutions for non-commissioned officers are limited to the infantry arm. During this period, it must be extended to all arms and special arms. Special education teams for officer candidates will be newly established in each regiment. This work has been carried out and promoted since October 1932.

Training Technical Soldiers 40

Heavy artillery and engineer teams have many tasks and work. According to their functions, the system of organization and leadership should be reorganized, and their work should be clearly divided. In addition to the platoons in the railway team, separate education units will be established to carry out the education of supplementary soldiers. New wireless radio teams will be established in the communications team, and specialists will be assigned to each division to carry out their special combat training (Dispatch from the China United Press on the 10th)

De Valera Plans to Propose Amendments to the Constitution to Parliament 43

Havas, Dublin, 9th The head of the executive branch of the Irish Free State is preparing to submit three draft laws on amending the constitution to the House of Representatives as soon as it convenes after the recess. The first bill abolishes the power of the British monarch's representative to reject bills. The second bill transfers the power of the British monarch's representative over appropriations to the Free State government. The third bill terminates the right of appeal to the British Privy Council and establishes the Free State Supreme Court as the final appellate court. If these three proposals become law, the office of governor-general will eventually be abolished, and all relations between Ireland and the British monarch will cease to exist.

Avoiding Assassination by German National Socialists

Professor Einstein recently lived in Belgium, and rumors have been rife that German secret societies have sent people to assassinate him. Although this claim has been denied by Berlin, the Belgian authorities have increased the number of secret agents to protect his safety. Professor Einstein and his wife initially planned to go out on a friend's yacht, but they have now changed their plans. Professor Einstein has many friends in England. Havas, London, 10th According to the Sunday Express, Professor Einstein, threatened by the German National Socialist Party's secret court [Vehmgericht], will come to England from Belgium to take refuge and arrived here last night. (Note: The Vehmgericht was a German secret court in the 15th century, which wielded considerable power. All tyrannical rulers and warriors who lived by pillage were feared.)

Leader of Spanish Radical Party Ordered to Attempt Formation of New Cabinet 86

Madrid dispatch, 9th. Tonight, Lerroux, leader of the Spanish Radical Party, accepted President Zamora's invitation to form a cabinet, and attempt to find new approach for the newly established republic. It is believed that the President hopes to preserve the present National Assembly, and attempt to get cooperation from all parties. It is reported that Lerroux, after taking office, will slightly relax restrictions on Catholic church, especially to repeal the law that deprive 80,000 monks and nuns from teaching in schools, to lower the opposition from the church. However, the socialist party leader claimed a month ago, that if a government is reorganised and ignores the party, they will resort to revolution. Whether Lerroux can get socialist's cooperation is doubted by many, but the President, seeing the increasing disappointment in the country, and after almost neglecting food and sleep due to anxiety, he is convinced that the new prime minister can save the situation. Although ex-Prime Minister Azaña has the support of 112 socialist National Assembly members, he alienated the church and radicals because his approach was too harsh, and will have to leave political stage for now. As the country was unstable in early June, the President worried about class conflict, so he hinted Azaña to resign and invited Lerroux to form a cabinet. The hope was that a compromise can be reached between radical and socialist parties, because the radical party, led by Lerroux, is relatively stable. However, Lerroux did not want to work with the socialists, so the President invited Azaña to form a cabinet again, and let him do it independently. However, the situation did not improve afterwards. In August, Azaña's government arrested 500 royalists and corporatists, accusing them of plotting to overthrow the republic. He was laughed at by all sides, and public support declined further. As the church opposed him for confiscating its properties and restricting its activities, the conservatives criticised him for only talking about policies instead of being a constructive leader, and the radicals did not like his actions, he had to resign eventually. It is rumoured that this resignation, like the previous one, was due to the President's insinuation. However, as Azaña was friendly to the Catalonians, the leaders in Barcelona were worried that Lerroux may not be as friendly to the Catalonia autonomous region.

Public Telegram 87

Kaifeng Telegram. All newspapers please note, Henan province has been suffering from disaster and bandits repeatedly, and the people are impoverished and in dire straits. This year in August, the Yellow River overflowed, exceeding the usual level by more than ten feet. The north and south riverbanks have broken simultaneously. According to reports, the counties of Hua, Mengjin, Kaocheng, Meng, Wen, Wuzhi, Fanshui, Lanfeng, Yucheng, Fengqiu, Guangwu, Kaifeng, Zhongmu, Chenliu, Zheng, Yuanwu, Jiyuan, Gong, Lingshi, and Qinyang, etc., are flooded, and there is a vast expanse of water. The plains have become wetlands. As the water came very suddenly, there was no time to prepare. Some cities have been completely flooded, and some embankments have been completely washed away. The old, the weak, women, and children have perished in the waves, and countless have died. Livestock, food, houses, tools, and crops have all been lost to the floods. The losses are incalculable. Those who were able to escape and be rescued have nowhere to stay and are suffering from hunger and cold, crying everywhere. The severity and extent of the disaster are unprecedented in recent decades. Winter is approaching soon, and without clothing or food, life will be even more difficult. Those who are wandering in the ditches are already a terrible sight. Those who are driven to desperation may cause harm to the area. Zhenhua and others are local people and are heartbroken by this catastrophe. We cannot reverse the tide, but we wish to call on others for help. We have always admired your compassion and earnestly request you to show great mercy and work together to do good deeds. Either generously donate from your wealth, or widely solicit relief, or introduce charitable individuals to provide aid, or widely publicize to all parties, in the hopes of doing as much good as possible and saving as many lives as possible. This will turn barren land into fertile land and bring immeasurable blessings. Urgent plea. We hope for your understanding. Liu Zhenhua, Zhang Fang, Liang Guanying, Liu Maoen, respectfully request your consideration.

Yu Xuezhong Arrives in Beiping 88

–Planning for Emergency Relief in the War Zone–

–Proceeding with the Takeover of Yuguan–

Beiping Correspondence. Yu Xuezhong of the Hebei Provincial Government returned to Tianjin from Beijing the day before yesterday. Yesterday (8th) afternoon at 4:00 PM, he arrived in Beiping on a special train, arriving at the East Station at 7:05 PM. Yu made the following statement at the station: "I was summoned by telegram by Chairman Chiang some time ago and left Beijing in mid-September, turning south to Pingnan. After arriving at Guling, I met with Chiang several times. Chiang inquired in detail about the situation in North China. After leaving Jiangxi, I went to Beijing to meet with Chairman Lin and President Wang. After completing these matters, I returned north. The urgent task in Hebei is emergency relief in the war zones of eastern Luan and northern Ji. I plan to convene a meeting immediately to actively proceed with this. As for the proposed issuance of 4 million relief bonds, the issuance period is not yet determined because the Legislative Yuan has not passed the bond regulations. The financial problem in Hebei is that the troops stationed in the province in recent years have exceeded three to four times the number in previous years, and the local burden is too heavy. The central government and Minister Song have agreed that the shortfall can be requested from the central government for assistance. I am currently instructing the Finance Department to prepare a budget for submission to the central government. Although the banditry in eastern Luan is very rampant, the rumor that the number of bandits in the area has reached 20,000 is inaccurate. Regarding the issue of sending troops to eastern Luan to suppress the bandits, after contacting the Japanese military headquarters, the Japanese side has no problems. However, the number of troops to be sent is not yet determined. The number of security teams stationed in the counties of eastern Luan is too small, and the training of special police is urgent. It has been decided that the provincial government will start training them, with a quota of 9,000, to be distributed to various parts of eastern Luan to undertake guard duties. Regarding the issue of the takeover of Lin Yu County, after Commissioner Liu Shisun contacted the matter in Tianjin, the Japanese side has agreed to begin withdrawing immediately. The Japanese puppet organizations in Yu City can be taken over recently. The withdrawal of Japanese troops from the five passes of the Great Wall is also currently under negotiation. Regarding the selection of the mayor of Tianjin, I have not heard of the rumor that the central government has internally decided on He Jingwu, so I think it is inaccurate. I am scheduled to visit Commissioner He tomorrow (9th) morning to report on my trip south and discuss the issue of bandit suppression in eastern Luan. Yu went to Jurentang at 9:30 this morning (9th) to visit He, reported on his trip south, and left after talking for about an hour. He went to the Foreign Affairs Building to attend a meeting of the emergency relief group of the North China War Zone Relief Committee. As Prince Carl of Sweden is scheduled to go to Tianjin this morning (9th), the Hebei Provincial Government is scheduled to host a banquet to welcome him at 8:00 PM, so Yu returned to Tianjin on the original special train at 1:40 PM this afternoon to facilitate the reception. He plans to come to Beiping again in the next few days to comprehensively plan for the suppression of bandits in the war zone and the takeover of various passes of the Great Wall in order to proceed. Yu also told reporters at the station, "Regarding the issue of bandit suppression in the war zone, Receiving Commissioner Yin Tong has dispatched personnel to Changchun to contact the Kwantung Army. Once negotiations are completed, our side will send security police to suppress them. Japanese troops are still stationed at the major passes of the Great Wall, and we will be able to take them over after negotiations. Shi Yousan arrived in Tianjin some time ago, and Hu Xie Wu, the leader of Shi's troops, has also arrived in Tianjin. Hu used to work in my Eighth Division, so he can also be said to be one of my old subordinates. Now, after persuasion from various parties, Hu and others have become aware of their mistakes and are willing to prioritize the concept of the country. The issue of the reorganization of Shi's troops will be entirely handled by Hu. The regulations on the administrative inspectors of the war zone have been submitted to the central government for review, but no reply has been received yet. It is not yet known whether Yin Rugeng's resignation as an inspector is true. The War Zone Relief Committee's emergency relief group met this morning, but the meeting was adjourned due to insufficient attendance. During the meeting, someone informally proposed that the relief work in Chahar Province be jointly handled with Hebei Province, but considering that the disaster in Hebei Province occurred first and the importance and urgency of the matter, it seems appropriate to handle them separately to avoid hindering each other."

Receiving Commissioners of the War Zone, Yin Tong, Liu Shisun, Tao Shangming, etc., previously visited He Yingqin to request instructions on all issues regarding the dispatch of troops to eastern Luan to suppress bandits and the takeover of the various passes of Yuguan Great Wall.

Page 10

It was decided that Yin et al. would continue to work with the Japanese to handle these issues. Liu Shisun went to Tianjin some time ago to negotiate with Kohtarō Nakamura, the food officer of the Japanese garrison, and plans to go to Yuguan within a day or two to negotiate with the local Japanese troops, returning to Beiping within a week. Tao Shangming also went to Tianjin the day before yesterday to negotiate with the Japanese and returned to Beiping yesterday morning (8th) to discuss everything at Jurentang. According to Tao, there is still no proper and concrete solution to the important issues of the Yuguan takeover and the dispatch of troops to eastern Luan to suppress bandits. Someone has been sent from here to Changchun to contact General Takashi Hishikari, commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army. The issue of the return of the various passes of the Great Wall is also being handled by someone in Changchun. Commissioner Liu (Shisun) went to Tianjin some time ago and will still go to Yuguan within a day or two. The banditry in eastern Luan is very rampant, and the people are living in misery. It is hoped that the government will take steps to eliminate it as soon as possible. Regarding emergency relief in the war zone, according to Zhang Yuanshan, director of the agricultural relief group of the War Zone Relief Association, "The agricultural relief funds have been decided to be 4 million in bonds issued by the Hebei Provincial Government, referring to the method used by the China International Famine Relief Commission to handle agricultural relief in Jiangxi and Anhui provinces last year. However, the regulations on the bonds have not yet been reviewed by the Legislative Yuan, so it is impossible to contact banks for sales. If it is delayed indefinitely, the spring ploughing next year will be delayed. The Northeast and Rehe Support Association previously allocated 93,000 yuan to the War Zone Relief Committee, which was transferred to this group. We are currently proceeding on a small scale. The agricultural relief areas are in eastern Luan, northern Ji, and southern Chahar, totaling 24 counties. We previously planned to send personnel to start with six counties first, with a period of two months, and the 24 counties will take a total of eight months. 84 field investigators are needed, and it has been decided that the Hebei Provincial Cooperative will select experienced personnel to fill the positions. This group recently hired 20 members from the cooperative, who are scheduled to gather in this group on the 15th of this month, and will then be given supplementary training for ten days. After the 25th of this month, they can set off, investigating while organizing mutual aid societies. Once the organization is complete, relief funds will be loaned out, and after one place is completely settled, they will proceed to other places." (9th)

Yellow River Flood in Henan Continues to Recede 89

Five Provinces Telegraph Request to Move Yellow River Commission Downstream

Henan Provincial Relief Committee Appeals for Relief by Telegraph

Kaifeng Correspondence. The Yellow River water level continues to drop significantly, and there seems to be no danger this year. The people of Bian are reassured, and discussions are gradually subsiding. Some time ago, the Civil Affairs Department sent Liu Zhangbo, the Finance Department sent Lu XieTang, the Construction Department sent Li Jichang, and the River Affairs Bureau sent Zhang Shaoyi to inspect the Hei Gang Kou river embankment. It is said that the cost of repairing the main embankment is 50,000 yuan, and the cost of repairing the polder embankment is 200,000 yuan. However, the funds have not yet been secured. Liu Zhi previously telegraphed the National Government and the Executive Yuan, requesting that the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission be moved to a central location downstream, and also telegraphed the chairmen of the four provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu, and Anhui, requesting a joint telegram. Now that they have replied with their consent, a telegram was sent to Lin and Wang today, and a provincial relief meeting was held to appeal to all parties to rescue those in distress. The texts of the telegrams are recorded below:

Telegram to the Government and Executive Yuan 90

Urgent. Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, President Wang of the Executive Yuan, in secret, examination of the Yellow River’s upstream does not reveal any prior disasters. From Mengjin downwards, to Lijin towards the ocean, the terrain is flat and sparse, and the river course is wide and dispersed. With a lack of silt, the riverbed rises several feet up to as much as two Zhang above the ground. During the Qing dynasty, the Yellow River breached in Henan 26 times; therefore the river supervisor at the time was located in Kaifeng to instruct with convenience, and command with dexterity. There are profound intentions. This time, the Yellow River swelled to an unprecedented level, causing widespread flooding. Still it occurred in the downstream. Now that the water has returned to its bed, the levees and dams on both banks are collapsing section by section. If we do not come up with methods to reinforce, then next year, with rising waters, the river will again flow uncontained and form another channel. The officials, examining previous disasters and considering current circumstances, believe that the Water Conservancy Commission, holding overall planning responsibility, with its headquarters far in Xijing, creates great inconvenience for surveying places where dangerous constructions might arise, planning, guiding engineering, or interim emergency repairs. The travel takes time. Therefore it is more appropriate that it be moved to a central location downstream so that it can take overall control of the river, so as not to miss opportunities. There is an agreement to request this together by telegram. Awaiting your approval and implementation, Chairman Gu Zhutong of Jiangsu, Chairman Han Fuqu of Shandong, Chairman Yu Xuezhong of Hebei, Chairman Liu Zhenhua of Anhui, and Chairman Liu Zhi of Henan, bow in obedience

Replies from the Various Provinces 91

(1) (Slightly omitted) Chairman Liu of Kaifeng, to brother Jingfu, with respect, the telegram is received and understood. Secretly, the current Yellow River flood is entirely in the downstream. I concur with the idea of moving the Water Commission to a downstream central location. Please draft and send the telegram with our names. Send a copy of the telegram for our records. Brother Liu Zhenhua, Ji Dong Zheng Yin. (2) (Slightly omitted) It is absolutely necessary to move the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission downstream. I concur with your excellent proposal. Please include my name in the telegram to appeal to the Central Government. Brother Han Fuqu, bow. Dong Shen Yin. (3) (Slightly omitted) The location of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission should be a suitable place in the downstream. I agree with the views expressed in your telegram. Please include my name and send the previous request again, and please send a copy for our records. Respectfully reply, brother Gu Zhutong, bow, Dong Mi Yin. (4) (Slightly omitted) I strongly agree with the relocation of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission downstream. Please add my name in the application. Brother Yu Xuezhong, bow. On behalf of the Minister of Civil Affairs, Wei Jian. Dong Zao Yin.

Provincial Relief Committee Telegram 92

The Provincial Relief Committee sent a telegram yesterday on behalf of Nanjing National Government Chairman Lin, General Commander Jiang in Guling, Nanjing Executive Yuan President and Minister of Internal Affairs, Chairman of the Relief Committee, and various charities in the North and South. (Titles omitted) Greetings. Henan Province, located in the Central Plains, is poor and barren, and in recent years, there have been disasters every year, leading to the desolation of the people's livelihood. Central Government and various charities in the North and South have provided generous assistance and relief. However, Heaven has not ceased to cause trouble, and disasters have piled on top of disasters. Due to a sudden, devastating flood of the Yellow River, the embankments in the counties of Kaocheng, Lanfeng, Huaxian, Mengjin, Fengqiu, Fanshui, Minquan, Kaifeng, Mengxian, Qinyang, Guangwu, Chenliu, Yucheng, Gongxian, Jiyuan, Wuzhi, Wenxian, Shangqiu, Xin'an, Shanxian, Mianchi, and Lingbao, etc., have collapsed, the river water has burst its banks, and the overflowing water has flowed horizontally, like wild horses. The torrential waves have arrived suddenly, collapsing villages and emptying turbid waves. Fields have been destroyed, the old and weak have been swept into the quicksand, and adults and children are trapped. Corpses have already begun to stink, young people climb to the roofs of houses and trees, suffering from hunger and cold, and their breath barely remains. Some cling to beams of wood and float, risking life and death amidst the waves, while others stand precariously and look into the distance, hoping for boats to come to their rescue. The suffering in the world is unbearable, and it is a pity for all to see. Now that the autumn wind is blowing and the summer is over, there are no houses to live in, no grains to eat, no clothes to wear, and no medicine to treat illness. The dead have already turned into insects in the sand, and the living are urgently seeking relief. Fields are full of such sights, and the organization is performing its duties day and night, but we lack funds. We hope that the Central Government and charitable people will share the sentiment of helping those in need and jointly rescue those who are starving and drowning. We ask for a donation to heal the root of the problem, or donate cotton clothing or purchase medicines, and send them out into the wind. The harvest will return to the fields. Remote decrees, disaster people continue their lives. We send the telegram with hope. We bow our heads. Chairman Zhang Fang of the Henan Provincial Relief Committee. (September 7th)

Lu Representative's Journey to Beijing to Petition for Disaster Relief 93

丨He Siyuan, Ge Xiangyi, and Others Have Returned to Jinan丨

Jinan Dispatch: He Siyuan, Director of Education of Shandong Province, departed from Jinan for Beijing on the 1st of this month to meet with Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, to report on the disastrous floods in the province and earnestly request the allocation of funds for emergency relief. He then boarded the Pinghu Railway train on the evening of the 7th, heading north from Beijing, and arrived in Jinan at 7:00 AM today (the 8th). In the afternoon, around 3:00 PM, he went to the Provincial Government to meet with Han Fuqu to report on his journey to Beijing. Ge Xiangyi and other representatives from western Shandong, who had also gone to Beijing to petition for disaster relief, returned to Jinan with He Siyuan. They will return to Heze on the same day to report the situation in Beijing to the disaster victims and convey the central government's intentions. According to He Siyuan's account of his journey to Beijing, he stated: "After arriving in Beijing, I immediately visited President Wang Jingwei to report on the disaster situation in the province and earnestly request assistance. Wang replied that Shandong Province had suffered a severe flood, and the disaster was exceptionally severe, as he had seen in detail in the newspapers. When the representatives arrived in Beijing to meet with him, they wept and expressed their grievances, which were especially sincere. He had already decided to allocate funds for disaster relief and had first telegraphed the Shandong Provincial Government to allocate 500,000 yuan for emergency relief to avoid exchange procedures. These funds will be reimbursed after the central government has made proper arrangements. He dared to guarantee this with his personal integrity." From this, it is clear that the central government attaches great importance to the disaster situation in Shandong. Before leaving, Wang also instructed Peng Xuepei, the Director of the Political Affairs Department, to inform him that they would meet at 9:30 AM the next day (the 2nd) at the Executive Yuan to discuss emergency relief measures for western Shandong. Subsequently, that evening, he received a phone call from Peng, stating that Minister Song Ziwen was scheduled to arrive in Beijing on the 2nd, and there might not be time to meet, so the meeting was rescheduled for 6:00 PM on the 2nd. The next day, introduced by Tang Xiang, he visited Song at 5:00 PM on the 2nd to report on the disastrous situation in western Shandong and request urgent relief measures. The conversation lasted a long time, and it was almost 7:00 PM when he left Song's residence. Wang had already left the Yuan and returned home, leaving Peng Xuepei to wait to meet with them. At that time, he told him that Wang would be going to Lushan on the 3rd and might not be able to meet. Later, at 10:00 PM, Peng again told them that Wang, considering the earnestness of the representatives, had specially scheduled a meeting at the Yuan at 6:00 AM the next day (the 3rd). He, Zhang Weicun, Ge Xiangyi, and 14 other representatives from western Shandong, complied and went to pay their respects at that time, reporting everything. Representative Ge Xiangyi also recounted the disastrous situation and the differences between the Yellow River and the Yangtze River situations. The Yangtze River flows slowly and is lower than the dikes. At most, there is only the risk of overflow, and the people of Jiangnan have many boats, so disasters are not a problem. The Yellow River is different, the river flows rapidly and the water is higher than the embankments, as well as several counties. Furthermore, Shandong has never had a breach, and each disaster originates in Hebei Province. He also requested that the central government coordinate the entire plan to manage the Yellow River and prevent floods in North China. Wang expressed deep agreement with his views. Wang also said that the Yellow River Conservancy Commission was established in 1928, with Feng Yuxiang as the chairman, but there were no results for several years, only a false reputation. Later, Zhu Qinglan was appointed as the chairman, and the same was true after several years. Although it was directly under the National Government at that time, there was practically no work done. Therefore, this reorganization is purely focused on practical work, with the appointment of water conservancy expert Li Yizhi as the chairman, and technical specialists from all parties as members and other important officials, and directly under the Executive Yuan to facilitate the progress of the project. The commission's major task is to unify the Yellow River system and formulate a fundamental plan for river management. As for the actual work, it still depends on the joint efforts and cooperation of the provincial governments. The central government has decided to actively raise funds for disaster relief in western Shandong and the Yellow River disaster area. With Minister Song's return to the country, it should not be difficult to raise these funds. The funds advanced by the provincial governments should be reimbursed immediately. At 4:00 PM that afternoon, the Yellow River Flood Relief Association held a standing committee meeting. He and others visited Liu Ruiheng, the acting chairman, and Xi Wujiu, the chief of the engineering department of the association, to discuss the situation of the flood in western Shandong in detail. Xi showed him a map of the disaster area in western Shandong, which was mostly inaccurate, and they pointed out the corrections. At 8:00 PM on the 4th, they met again at Liu Ruiheng's private residence, and also met with Mei Yilin and others. Regarding disaster relief, it was decided that the Central Relief Commission would directly send personnel to the north to provide relief with the remaining 3 million yuan, adopting a district-based, not province-based approach, to eliminate regional boundaries. Liu Ruiheng decided to send Mei Yilin to western Shandong first to survey the disaster. He immediately telegraphed Chairman Han to send senior officials to accompany Mei on the survey, to show sincerity in attaching importance and assisting. While in Beijing, he informed all parties in the central government that Shandong Province would ensure the speed, integrity, and absence of other problems in disaster relief, whether it be food, transportation, or relief personnel. At the meeting of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, the situation of the disaster in Shandong was understood to be manageable.

Inspection Report of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei by Our Newspaper's Special Correspondent, Ren An 94

Liling County Town and Villages

Liling Special Dispatch: It is traditionally said that there is a hill north of Liling County, and at the foot of the hill is a well with a spring as sweet as liqueur, hence the name of the county. Today, there is still a stone-built square well outside the North Gate, with a stone tablet covered in moss standing beside it, inscribed with the four characters "Liqueur Spring Immersing the Moon," which are powerful and impressive. It is said that this well is also one of the "Eight Scenic Spots of the Lu River," but the water storage is very shallow, like a small pond, and sometimes it dries up, so the spring is no longer visible today. The county town is located on both banks of the Lu River, with the South Gate on the south bank of the river, and the remaining three gates on the north bank. Connecting the traffic between the two banks is the Lu River Bridge, which is more than two zhang wide and more than thirty zhang long. The river comes from the east, encircles the south and west, and Jiangling stands towering to the north, so the city has the momentum of relying on the mountains and facing the water. The ancients had the lines "The mountain is low and connected to the shore, the sound of the river curves around the city," and "People everywhere live by the water, opening the window to sit and watch the mountains," which can truly be said to be poems for the city.

Liling's transportation is convenient by both water and land. The Zhuping and Yuehan railways pass through the county. The ordinary express train that the reporter took from Jiangxi to Liling, which transported both coal and passengers, was very slow and poorly equipped. The station name signs were mostly collapsed, making it difficult for passengers to identify their destination when getting off the train.

Laoguan, also known as Chalingguan, is an important place where Jiangxi and Hunan meet. The scenery seen after passing through the pass into Hunan is very different from that of Jiangxi, which can't help but make people feel moved. The farmers seen are mostly strong men with full expressions. Recalling the villages in Jiangxi, most of them were old and weak people. When spoken to, they seemed to turn a deaf ear, but on closer inspection, they seemed to contain infinite pain. Compared with the Hunan farmers with full expressions, they were completely different. Moreover, there were no soldiers checking luggage when entering Liling City. The people in the market were bustling and lively, and the business district was full of vitality. It is undoubtedly a happy land. However, reading the local Minbao and Lujiang Xingbao, border bandit police reports are still occasionally heard. The county government and local public groups have enacted and promulgated numerous and strict laws and regulations regarding the pacification of bandits by the Baojia system. Violation is punishable by beheading and collective punishment, and shooting is only secondary. It is said that in the years 1927 and 1928, the bandits who were killed numbered in the dozens every day, totaling about 6,000 people, including more than 60 students, especially young people aged 13 or 14. The farmers in the southern district were deeply banditized, and men were killed when they were suppressed. Many people fled abroad, resulting in a severe shortage of men in the area for a time.

According to Director Pan of the Education Bureau, the education situation is that the funds received are 15,000 piculs of grain rent, worth about 20,000 yuan, about 20,000 yuan in additional taxes, and 10,000 yuan in deed taxes, totaling about 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. The expenses are also the same. When the price of grain is low, it is not enough. There are also district funds, and the annual income also increases and decreases from time to time. The county has one normal school and one women's normal school, each with one or two classes attached to the middle school, 15 higher primary schools, and originally 900 lower primary schools, but now there are only 700 schools. The low price of grain not only affects education but also the local production, which will shrink day by day. Taking the grain itself as an example, the cost of each stone is about three yuan, but the selling price is no more than two yuan. The farmers' hard work for a year results in harm to them. From then on, farming is casual, and more planting means more loss, and less planting means a sharp decline in production. Both are harmful to the farmers, and the hidden worries of society are truly unimaginable.

Liling's products have always been known for their abundance: (1) Porcelain. The porcelain clay in the county extends for dozens of miles. The kilns for manufacturing porcelain originally numbered 13, namely, Model, Cooperative, Minli, Heji, Yuhua, Improved, Shunye, Dehou, Tianbao, Minsheng, Zhonghe, Jiuru, and Chuli factories. Each factory fired three kilns a month, for ten months a year, worth more than 300,000 yuan. The total value of each factory reached three to four million yuan. The amount sold to other provinces was about three million yuan. Recently, due to the stagnation of the rural economy, sales have decreased sharply. Each factory now produces only one-third of its original output, and there is still a mountain of goods. The Jiuru and Chuli factories have already closed down, and the remaining eleven factories, as well as more than 20 local porcelain factories that are struggling to survive, are also in a precarious situation. The total number of workers who rely on the porcelain industry for their livelihood, directly and indirectly, is 200,000, which is equivalent to one-third of the county's population. Now, they are also gradually becoming unemployed in large numbers. The county government is deeply concerned that these workers will have nothing to eat and will increase the number of vagrants in society, creating new bandits in the area. Recently, it has specially loaned 10,000 yuan of working capital to each factory in the hope of restoring the old business, but with little porridge and many monks, it is doubtful whether it can provide widespread relief. It is noted that Liling porcelain has always had a good reputation. In 1909, the Nanyang Industrial Exhibition was held in Nanjing, and Liling porcelain went to compete and won a first-class gold medal, ranking above Jingdezhen. If it is further improved and refined, it can also resist foreign porcelain. For the sake of maintaining national rights and interests and people's livelihood, the government must have a way to maintain it. (2) Tea. In the past, Liling tea was exported abroad, worth hundreds of thousands of yuan a year. Later, due to the mixing of miscellaneous leaves, its reputation fell. Today, the tea used is imported from Pingxiang and Youxian. Improvements have recently been promoted, but the results are not yet obvious. (3) Summer cloth. The quality is the best in the country, with annual exports worth about 70,000 to 80,000 yuan, but now sales are sluggish, and it has fallen to about 300,000 yuan. (4) Indigo. Before the rise of foreign indigo, this county and Pingtan and other places all obtained their supplies from this. Since the invasion of foreign indigo, the price of indigo has plummeted, and many farmers have abandoned planting it. If the manufacturing is not improved and domestic products are not promoted, it will soon become extinct.

The reporter was invited by his friend Mr. Zhang to visit the villages in the eastern countryside. Going up the Lu River, the trees are lush, and the fragrance of rice is refreshing. The scenery is pleasant, and I forget the hardships of the journey. The mountain villages are densely populated, and there is little abandoned land. Rice is divided into early and late crops. The late rice planted among the rows of early rice is called Yahe, also known as Erhe. The late rice planted after the early rice is harvested is called Fanzi, also known as Shun (it is taboo to say Fan, so it is said backwards). In addition to applying manure and lime, fertilizer is also made by inserting cigarette butts into the roots of the rice, which is quite peculiar. Most of the farmers are tenant farmers, accounting for more than 80% of the population. Liling County originally had many large landlords with more than a thousand stones of land. Recently, in order to avoid attracting attention to the term "large landlord," there have been many cases of fathers and sons and brothers dividing the property and managing it. The price of land, which was previously worth more than 200 yuan per dou (about one mu), is now sold for 70 to 80 yuan, but there are still no takers. It is said that each surname has a family temple, but the system has been abandoned to the extreme. Commander Liu of the garrison is doing his best to promote and restore the old rules, but no one dares to take the lead because they are afraid that the Red Army will regard them as feudal elements. In the main hall of the residences, there are shrines dedicated to Heaven, Earth, Emperor, Parents, and Teacher, or the word "Emperor" is changed to "Country" or "Honor." Next to it are the ancestral tablets, the Earth God, and other gods. Every village and community must have a community god, called the Great King, each with a different title. Their images are mostly sculpted as armed soldiers in armor. It is said that during the Yuan Dynasty, Mongol soldiers were stationed in every ten households to monitor the local people and were called the Great King. The accumulated hatred was deep, so they agreed to get the Mongols drunk on the night of the Mid-Autumn Festival and kill them all at the same time, calling it killing the Tartars. After killing them, they were afraid that they would become malevolent spirits, so they worshiped them in the temple of the community god and called it the Great King Temple. The secret code for agreeing to kill the Tartars at that time was called "Reporting Spring." The reporter of spring always held a red paper, on which was drawn a picture of a person following an ox, titled "Sending the Spring Ox to Your Home, Everything is Flourishing and Enjoying Glory, Four Seasons of Good Weather, Generations of Children and Grandchildren Rich and Noble." The paper is sent to each household and must be rewarded appropriately. This custom is still followed today. The reporter visited several of Mr. Zhang's relatives and friends. Upon entering the door, the host was courteous and enthusiastic. In addition to offering cigarettes, tea, cakes, and fruits, the hostess also offered her homemade chili peppers (soaked in salt) to entertain the guests, which tasted quite good, but those who were not accustomed to eating chili peppers could not stand it.

Liling was formerly known as a remote county, and its people were very conservative. Since the rise of the military, many farmers have abandoned their hoes to join the army. They support each other, and the number of people who go out to make a living is increasing day by day. The number of people who have risen through military exploits is also increasing day by day. He Jian, the current commander-in-chief of the Western Route and chairman of Hunan Province, Liu Jianxu, the commander of the 28th Army, Tao Guang, the commander of the 62nd Division, Zhong Guangren, the deputy brigade commander, Chen Mingren, the deputy commander of the 80th Division, Yan Guotao, the commander of the 6th Security District, Deng Wenyi, the staff secretary of the Military Commission, Yi Shuzhu, the secretary-general of the Fourth Route Headquarters, and Zhang Kailian, the director of the Hunan Provincial Finance Department, are all from Liling. In the past, the villagers felt that Chiang Kai-shek cared about his hometown (Fenghua, Zhejiang) and paid attention to education and construction. They had discussed that Chairman He should follow Chiang's example and voluntarily donate a large sum of money to establish a Yunqiao (He's pseudonym) school in the county town so that children of commoners could attend school for free. (September 2nd)

Tragedy in the Pear Garden: Liu Xiaoheng's Blood Stains the Stage 95

=Assailant Mounts the Stage and Stabs During Performance=

=Supporting Actor Zhang Wenyuan Also Stabbed Simultaneously=

=The Assailant Unable to Escape, Commits Suicide on the Spot=

Tianjin Dispatch: Celebrated Dan (female role) Liu Xiaoheng is the son of the late Tongchui Hualian (painted face role) Liu Yongchun. He initially performed as Laosheng (old male role) without much renown. Later, he switched to Huashan (florid shirt, a type of female role), achieving great fame. Among Huashan roles in Shanghai, he was one of the top figures. His performance in the play "The Civet Cat for the Crown Prince" was popular overseas, a piece co-created by Xiaoheng and the well-known Wusheng (martial male role) Chang Chunheng. During the January 28th Incident and the Shanghai War, Xiaoheng also found it difficult to recover his situation for a time. He took a steamer north and performed in Yantai, Qingdao, Dalian, and other places. This spring, he was again hired by Dalian to perform at the Xishangang Grand Stage, with excellent results. All the supporting actors in Xiaoheng's plays were people who had been with him for many years. One small Hualian actor joined his troupe when Xiaoheng arrived in Dalian, playing a supporting role. In April of this year, Xiaoheng was invited by a theater in Andong to perform for two months. This small Hualian actor also accompanied him. After the contract expired, Liu dismissed him because he acted too rigidly and could not enhance the performance. Liu's Qinyin (stringed instrument) player recommended another small Hualian actor as a replacement. The father of the dismissed small Hualian actor worked as a Jianchang (stage checker) at the Xishangang Grand Stage. He was very resentful because his son was dismissed by Liu. Furthermore, he resented even more because the small Hualian actor who was now performing with Xiaoheng was recommended by Liu's Qinyin player. Little did anyone know that a murderous intent was brewing.

The stage checker, surnamed Mou, was extremely anxious because his son was unemployed. He decided to kill Liu and Liu's Qinyin player, as well as the small Hualian actor currently performing with Liu, to vent his anger. He specially purchased an extremely sharp Japanese sword and hid it in his sleeve. One evening a week ago, Xiaoheng was performing "Wulongyuan Kills Xi" with Yang Ruiting and the small Hualian actor. The stage checker secretly drew his sharp blade and stood inside the stage door. No one backstage noticed. When Song Jiang called for the door and Yan Poxi ordered Zhang Wenyuan to temporarily avoid him, walking into the backstage from the back entrance, (according to this play, Xiaoheng plays Yan Poxi, Ruiting plays Song Gongming, and the small Hualian actor plays Zhang Wenyuan,) the stage checker took advantage of his unpreparedness and suddenly stabbed him in the abdomen with his blade. The small Hualian actor screamed in extreme pain and fainted on the spot. When the backstage crew saw the murder, they rushed to rescue him. Taking advantage of the confusion, the stage checker ran to the front stage with the blade. At this time, Xiaoheng was still in dialogue with Ruiting and was unaware of the tragedy that had occurred backstage. When he saw the stage checker running out with a steel knife covered in blood, he knew something was wrong. Before he could escape, the blade had entered Xiaoheng's abdomen. Fortunately, Yang Ruiting was a Wusheng actor and reacted quickly. He pushed the man with great force, reducing the impact of the strike. When the knife was pulled out, Xiaoheng was covered in blood. After being stabbed, Xiaoheng said loudly, "What hatred do I have with you that you dare to commit such a violent act?" When he lowered his head and saw the fresh blood gushing from his abdomen, he let out a cry and fell to the stage. After stabbing Xiaoheng, the stage checker took his knife to the prop table, intending to kill Liu's Qinyin player to complete his planned murder. When he saw that the person playing the instrument was not Xiaoheng's Qinyin player but Ruiting's assistant, he stomped his feet and shouted, "What a cheap son of a bitch!" Seeing the leading actor stabbed and lying on the stage covered in blood, the front and back stage crew hurriedly carried Xiaoheng backstage.

The assailant, seeing that he had killed two of his three enemies, attempted to escape. He saw that he was surrounded on all sides, with armed police standing in front of the stage with guns, and the martial arts performers in the troupe blocking the upper and lower stage doors with weapons. They all shouted for him to throw away the murder weapon and surrender quickly. Seeing the situation, he knew he could not escape. He let out a loud laugh, held the blade against his own neck, and with a powerful stroke, his head rolled off with the knife. His body then fell to the stage.

There were many spectators in the theater that evening. Just as they were enjoying the art of Liu and Yang, they suddenly witnessed the tragedy. The order was completely disrupted, and people rushed to escape, destroying tables and chairs and shattering tea sets. Countless people were挤傷 (squeezed and injured), 摔傷 (fell and injured), 跌傷 (tripped and injured), 踏傷 (trampled and injured), 碰傷 (bumped and injured), and 撞傷 (collided and injured).

Seeing that the assailant had committed suicide, the front and back stage crew first set about rescuing the two injured men. They quickly had a car send them to a foreign hospital for treatment. After examining Xiaoheng, the hospital said that his large intestine had been severely injured. They first used anesthesia to make Liu unconscious, then cut open his abdomen and treated the stabbing wounds. After sewing him up with medicated thread and using chicken skin to seal the wound, the doctor said that if there were no other complications within a week, his life could be saved. The small Hualian actor also relied on the strength of the chicken skin to seal the wound. Last night, a performer came to Tianjin from Dalian, saying that Liu and the others' injuries were improving and that there should be no accidents.

Murder cases in the Pear Garden have been endless for more than 20 years, but they usually occurred either inside the residence or on the way home after the performance. This time, to be brutally murdered while performing on stage is unprecedented. (September 7th)

Songjiang 96

Woman from Jiangbei Deceived and Hangs Herself

A woman was found hanging in the Kui Xing Pavilion across the river from the West Temple of Literature in this city yesterday (the 9th) evening. Her limbs were already stiff, and there was no way to save her. The woman appeared to be dressed as someone from Jiangbei. Many people from Jiangbei live in this area, gathering to cultivate land and growing vegetables to make a living. After the town police investigated house by house, it was discovered that she was Wu Quanzhen's wife, Wu Pan, from Jiangbei. She was 30 years old and had a 10-year-old son. She usually saved every penny and accumulated 190 yuan through hard work. Wang Guilin, a fellow villager, deceived her by saying that they would jointly purchase several acres of wasteland and cultivate it together. The woman was seduced by the prospect of great profits and handed over the money, agreeing on a date for the transfer. However, when the date arrived, Wang Guilin was nowhere to be found. When asked, the landlord denied the matter. The woman realized that she had been deceived and was extremely distraught. Overcome with resentment, she sought this short end. Her husband has reported the matter to the authorities for an inquest and is preparing for the funeral.

Suzhou 97

Military Officer Kills Wife and Then Commits Suicide

Zhong Xunqi, a Hunan native and former junior military officer, lived with his wife, Su Zhen, at No. 7 Balian Bridge in Chaimanwai. The couple was in their twenties and had a very close relationship. On the afternoon of the 9th, the couple went out together and returned home around 7:00 PM. A conflict suddenly arose, but it quickly subsided. Around midnight that night, Yu Qichang, a servant of the Zhang family who lived with them, suddenly heard a terrible cry from Zhong's room. Knowing something was wrong, he immediately called another resident, Zhang Heshang, and they planned to push the door open to see what was happening. However, at that moment, the lights in the room suddenly went out. They lit a candle and entered, only to find Zhong and his wife lying in a pool of blood. A kitchen knife was left beside Zhong. They reported it to the police station, who sent police to the scene to investigate. The two were already dead. When the tragedy occurred, the light wire in their room was cut, causing all the lights in the house to go out. On the morning of the 10th, they reported to the court to come for an inquest. Unexpectedly, Zhong, whose throat had not been completely severed, suddenly revived. He secretly took a kitchen knife from the residence and madly rushed out, slashing at anyone he encountered. Passersby fled in all directions. The police chased after him, but Zhong ran straight to Xiajin Bridge and jumped into the river. He was pulled out, already dead. In the afternoon, the judge conducted an autopsy. The autopsy revealed that Zhong had only one wound to his throat from the self-inflicted cut. His wife, Su Zhen, had her right wrist severed, and there were many knife wounds on her private parts, legs, and neck. It appeared that Zhong killed his wife and then committed suicide due to an affair. Since there were no relatives, there was no way to know the truth. The local police were instructed to prepare a coffin and await further investigation.

Wuxi 98

Striving Against the Province to Retain County Funds

The Public Funds and Public Property Management Office of this county previously received an official letter from the county government, forwarding instructions from the Jian Ting, ordering that 8,100 yuan for the provincial-level agricultural, forestry, silkworm, and fishery fields located in Xiyi, 2,700 yuan for the salaries and expenses of industrial guidance technicians, should still be remitted monthly from May of this year, in accordance with the Ting's instructions. After receiving the letter, the office believed that since self-government was based on the county as a unit, all undertakings should also be based on the county. The special funds for industry in each county mainly came from the two-cent per mu donation for agricultural improvement levied since 1929. The original plan for provincial Ting collection had been repeatedly ordered and strictly prohibited from being used for other purposes. It was to be used specifically for agricultural improvement in each county, with detailed budgets that could not be mixed up. The county's undertakings were endless, and the county's funds were only insufficient. If the development of county undertakings was to be sought, it would still depend on the provincial funds to supplement it. Now, the agricultural improvement mu donation, which was levied specifically for each county since 1929, was being taken for the expenses of provincial undertakings, ignoring the established case of 1929. This created the suspicion of mixing provincial and county affairs, greatly affecting local finances. Moreover, after reviewing the local budget for 1933, it was truly impossible to allocate from it. Therefore, they specially sent a letter to the county government yesterday, requesting that it be forwarded to the provincial Ting to investigate and determine which expenses under the budget item should be used in detail to facilitate compliance.

Director of Education Bureau Accused 99

Since Zang Hulu came to the Education Bureau, he stopped allocating funds to the privately run Dunmu Elementary School in Xiangxiangbang, South Township of this county. The school board of directors repeatedly sent people to negotiate, and he agreed to maintain the funds. Later, it was discovered that Director Zang had falsely claimed and embezzled the school's funds. The school board of directors reported the matter to the provincial and county governments, requesting a thorough investigation to rectify the situation. However, in July of this year, Director Zang stopped allocating all of the school's funds. The association believed that Director Zang did not understand the situation and that because they had exposed his private matters, he was ashamed and angry. He did not hesitate to distort the official documents to suppress them, wantonly destroy the school, and arbitrarily stop the allocation of regular funds, putting the school to death as revenge. Yesterday, they specifically prepared a document presenting the situation of the Education Bureau's suspension of regular funds and the accumulated losses to the provincial Ting for verification and defense.

Nantong 100

Provincial Second Regiment Receives Transfer Notice Like a Sea

The Provincial Security First Regiment, stationed in Tongruhai, departed for Zhenjiang on the 9th. The Second Regiment will cross the Yangtze River from Jiangnan within days to take over the defense. The Security Office telegraphed Commissioner Ye of the Seventh District, saying, "The First Regiment has been stationed for a long time. Now, the regiment will be transferred to Zhenjiang on a scheduled date for centralized training. The defense duties of Nantong, Haimen, Rugao, and other areas left behind have been ordered to be taken over by the Second Regiment. Before the Second Regiment arrives, you are to instruct the county governments to assign团警 (regiment police) to temporarily maintain order."

Hydrographic Bureau Measures Qingtian Reef 101

The Qingtian Reef on the Nantong River has recently seen a growth of surrounding sandbars, and the water flow has changed direction. The Hydrographic Bureau of the Naval Department has sent the Jiao Ri surveying ship to Tong for surveying.

Gaoyou 102

Xia Jiazhang Shot Dead by Bandits

Twenty bandits suddenly came to the home of a farmer surnamed Shi in Zhuangxiang, the tenth district of the county. Each of them held various firearms. After looting, they bound Shi's son and took him away. When Xia Jiazhang heard the alarm, he bravely took up a gun and led the villagers to pursue the bandits. The bandits then opened fire to resist. Xia Jiazhang was shot in a vital spot and fell to the ground and died instantly. The bandits then fired more than ten shots into the air and fled with a whoop.

Jiangyin 103

A Village Woman Strangle to Death

Cui, the wife of Cai Zufu, a farmer from the Jinjia Village, Houmei Guantong Township, Sixth District, was suddenly dragged out of her room on the evening of the 7th and strangled to death with a rope. Her body was found in the river of Xiacun. Two suspects, Wang Wei and Da Wang Xifang, were apprehended at the time. The Sixth District Office delivered them to the county on the 8th. On the 9th, County Commissioner Shi Chen went to the village to conduct an on-site inspection.

Zhenjiang 104

Notorious Bandit Jiang Tiecheng Escorted to the Provincial Capital

Jiang Tiecheng, a notorious bandit from Yancheng, was previously involved in occupying lake embankments, kidnapping, killing, and plundering the local area, confiscating public firearms, aiding bandits, participating in joint kidnappings, dividing the spoils on the spot, and illegally manufacturing firearms.

Due to these various illegal activities, citizens such as Yu Ying and others filed charges. Dong Hancha, the Special Commissioner of the Tenth District and concurrently Magistrate of Yancheng County, arrested the bandit. After repeated interrogations, Jiang Tiecheng confessed without reservation. Dong then dispatched personnel yesterday afternoon to escort Jiang Tiecheng to the provincial capital and hand him over to the Security Department for legal proceedings.

Yangzhou 105

Three Girls Beat a Madman to Death

Bai Wennian's third son, a resident of Fangjia Lane Town in the northern countryside of the county, had reached the age of adulthood but suffered from occasional bouts of madness. The other day, he led an ox to graze in the graveyards behind the town. Coincidentally, three girls from Zhu Village, aged eight, nine, and twelve, were playing together. Bai's madness suddenly flared up, and he made frivolous advances. The girls, feeling insulted and extremely ashamed, pushed Bai to the ground and beat him severely. Unexpectedly, the wooden stick struck a vital spot, causing instant death. By the time his father, Wennian, rushed to the scene, it was too late to save him. He negotiated with the parents of the girls. As a result, Zhang Shixiang and others from the town's meat industry acted as mediators, providing 300 yuan for clothing, a coffin, and funeral expenses, and the matter was settled.

Huzhou 106

Cargo Ship from Huzhou to Xinshi Robbed

A night-shift cargo ship traveling from this city to Xinshi was fully loaded with goods and departed from Huzhou for Xinshi at approximately 6:00 PM on the 7th of this month. While passing through the Qianjin Taiping Bridge area, two bandit ships suddenly appeared with over a dozen robbers, each armed with a pistol. They forced the ship to stop. The bandits then boarded the ship and carried out a large-scale robbery, taking away 200 cartons of Golden Mouse brand cigarettes, two large boxes of Heavenly Bridge brand cigarettes, forty bolts of Yongbu cloth, four lengths of Huzhou silk, and items such as clothing and bedding, resulting in significant losses.

Workers at Dachang Factory Go on Strike 107

Workers at the Dachang Silk Weaving Factory in Huilong Bridge, Ximen, in this city, have initiated a strike due to the factory owner's wage cuts. The strike has lasted for ten days without resolution. Although the Wuxing Silk Weaving Guild and the Weaving Workers' Union have petitioned the county government for mediation, both sides have taken extreme positions, leading to no progress. The union has again petitioned the county government, requesting a second mediation within a short period. It is learned that the county government has approved a meeting to be convened on the afternoon of the 10th at 1:00 PM to resolve the issue.

Hefei 108

Bandit Gang Led by Zhang Big Nose Defeated

A bandit gang led by Zhang Big Nose, who had been causing trouble in Hanshan County, infiltrated the Huatangji and Guangxingji areas in Hefei on the 4th from Dongxi Huangshan and Xianzong, setting up bases and looting. The Hefei Security Brigade, which had been dispatched to Liangyuan Town to prevent them, received the alert. The Deputy Brigade Commander Wang Zhexing ordered them to advance in the rain and encircle the bandits. The bandits resisted fiercely. The battle raged until night, resulting in the death of over forty bandits, the rescue of over thirty kidnap victims, and the seizure of over ten donkeys, one bicycle, and over twenty firearms. The bandits, unable to withstand the pressure, fled into the sorghum fields under the cover of darkness, escaping southwest. The chase is ongoing. Wang Jun, the commander of the Third Army stationed in Lu'an, considering the bandit gang led by Zhang Big Nose had become a roving threat, dispatched Li Wenbin, the commander of the 21st Brigade of the 7th Division and concurrently the General Commander for Bandit Suppression in the border area of five counties, to Hefei on the evening of the 5th in six automobiles. He is scheduled to lead a large army within days to suppress them and pacify northern Anhui.

Mingguang 109

Flooding Caused by River Overflow

Since the beginning of autumn, there have been consecutive days of rain, causing mountain torrents and rising water levels in the Chi River. The water from the upper reaches, winding and turning, could not flow smoothly, leading to overflows. Land along the river, from Sanheji up to Maguozui, was flooded, affecting no less than a thousand acres. The crops nearing harvest were submerged.

Hearing Officer Replaced 110

Li Qiguang, the hearing officer of this county, has been transferred to the Anhui High Court. The vacant position will be filled by Ke Xiaojing, a hearing officer from Wuyuan. The handover between the old and new officers took place the day before yesterday.

Six Members of the Militia Killed in Action While Suppressing Bandits 111

Yesterday morning (the 5th), a group of fifty to sixty bandits suddenly arrived at the Zha Jiabu Fort north of the town. After occupying and looting the two villages of Da and Xiao Du, they advanced south with hostages, attempting to seize Zha Jiabu. The fort's militia went to intercept them. The battle raged until midnight, after which the bandits fled northeast. Six members of the militia, including Shen Zhilin, were killed in action, and two were injured. The Fifth District Office is in the process of raising funds for relief and compensation.

Local News

Jiangque Aircraft Refitting Completed 112

Today's Test Flight Fine, Depart this Afternoon

Can Reach Nanjing that Day, Transfer to Beiping Overnight

Chen Wenlin, Director of the Xiamen Naval Aviation Department, and Pan Dingxin, Chief of the Mechanical Section, previously piloted the self-made Jiangque aircraft on a long-distance flight across the country. After arriving in Shanghai, the engine was refitted. The work was completed last night. A test flight is scheduled for this morning, and the flight will continue this afternoon. Details are as follows.

Refitting Completed

After the Jiangque aircraft arrived in Shanghai from Xiamen via Nanjing, it landed at Hongqiao Airport. The original 85-horsepower engine was refitted to 120-horsepower. After setting up a shed at Hongqiao Airport, the refitting was carried out by Wang Dinghai and Wu Xishan, two craftsmen sent by the Xiamen Aviation Department, and two craftsmen sent by the Shanghai Naval Aircraft Department. Starting the day before, the Naval Aircraft Department added two more craftsmen to speed up the work, which was completed yesterday afternoon.

Depart Today

After the work was completed yesterday, Director Chen Wenlin is scheduled to conduct a test flight this morning. If he deems it satisfactory, he will continue the flight this afternoon with Section Chief Pan Dingxin to complete the planned long-distance flight across the country. After arriving in Nanjing that day, they will stay for one day. On the morning of the 12th, they will depart from Nanjing and are expected to arrive in Beiping that day via Jinan and Tianjin. After staying for two or three days, they will return to Tianjin from Beiping, transfer to Qingdao, and return to Shanghai. Then, they will depart from Shanghai again, passing through Hangzhou, Wenzhou, and Fuzhou to the Xiamen Aviation Department. They are scheduled to fly to Shantou, Hong Kong, Guangzhou, and Wuzhou to Liuzhou, and then fly to Hankou, transfer to Shanghai, and return to Xiamen.

Yesterday afternoon at 0:30, aviator Sun Tonggang gave a broadcast speech on the radio station at the Central Western Pharmacy on Fourth Road. Chen Tingzhen of the Central Western Pharmacy first gave an introduction, followed by Sun's speech. He stated that after the European War, countries around the world focused on military equipment and aviation construction. In France alone, there were more than 5,000 aircraft. The United Kingdom and the United States were also expanding significantly. Although Germany's quantity cannot be examined in detail due to treaty restrictions, the degree of its increase may not be lower than that of the great powers. After the failure of previous attempts to mediate world peace, countries have been increasingly preparing for war in the Pacific. The key instrument for future struggles will be the air force. Although our country has gradually begun to make efforts in this regard, it still lags behind the great powers by a factor of ten or twenty. I sincerely hope that the people of the country will work together to preserve the inherent glory of our nation and maintain the inherent territory of our country. Even the backwardness of Chinese culture, the desolation of the frontier, and the like, cannot be addressed without a great air force to bridge the gaps. Therefore, for the sake of the country and the nation, we must engage in the construction of the air force. The reason I flew back to China, encountering all kinds of dangers, was simply to make the compatriots in the country know what to strive for and what to advocate. As for personal donations of money, I only seek to benefit the public and the country and to win glory for our country. After the speech, Zhou Bangjun, the manager of the Central Western Pharmacy, delivered a farewell speech.
