Stopped Shipping from Yesterday Morning

Separate Letters to Each Line Stating Responsibility

Other Passengers and Cargoes are Loaded and Transported as Usual

The medicine stores and hotel division in this city, in order to oppose the Shantou gang's deduction of the strength and bottom water of the hotel, announced a strike from yesterday. The Shantou gang, Hongtai, completely stopped loading with passengers and cargo. The medicine industry trade union sent separate letters to the managers of each line stating the responsibility for the strike, and organized a temporary committee to take charge of everything. Other passengers and cargoes from each gang are still loaded and transported as usual. The situation of each branch is recorded as follows:

Statement of Responsibility

The Medicine Industry Trade Union sent separate letters to the managers of each medicine line yesterday, stating the responsibility for the strike. The original letter is recorded as follows: Dear Sirs, I have found that the case of the Shantou gang businessmen Hong Taixing, Lin Yiji, Datongchang, etc., for deducting the strength and bottom water of the hotel, has been repeatedly dispatched by the association. Lin Yiji and Datongchang need merchants and have made considerable statements, waiting to be resolved after informing the Shantou Chamber of Commerce. However, Hong Zizhao, a businessman from Hong Taixing, has a tough attitude. In addition to deducting the bottom water, he also changed the unit strength of 14 yuan within the prescribed limit to the calculation of foreign codes, deliberately destroying the workers' livelihood. This has reached its extreme, and if we do not deal with it severely, the cunning and stubbornness of the businessman will not be able to warn him in the future. Therefore, a temporary meeting was convened and resolved, and it was decided that from the 10th of this month, all the shops and inns would be notified to stop transporting Hong Taixing's medicinal materials, and to petition the party and government agencies to mediate, and to send a letter to the same industry office to find out and order a statement. In addition to the responsibility issue of stopping the transportation this time, I would like to ask you to inspect and take care of the Hehe.

Each Gang is As Usual

After the workers of the industry announced the strike yesterday, Hong Taixing's passengers and goods from the Shantou gang completely stopped transporting. However, passengers and goods from Guangzhou, Xiamen, Tianjin, Sichuan, Zhejiang, Tongzhou, and other gangs were transported as usual. The Shantou gang, in addition to Hong Taixing, the others such as Lin Yiji Datongchang, etc., were not affected.

Departing Investigation

Regarding all foreign and internal affairs during the strike period, it is recommended that the union directors Sang Yutang, supervisor Weng Dongsheng, and the directors of each share form a temporary committee to preside over the meeting, and send Li Minghua and other 17 people as investigators to set off separately to investigate whether there is any destructive behavior in the same industry.

[P Zhabei Silk Factory Still Stopped Work Yesterday>

Labor and Management Agreed to Start the Car This Morning

After the labor dispute in the silk factory in this city was resolved by the Social Affairs Bureau, the factories temporarily stopped the car in order to avoid unnecessary losses due to the repeated misunderstandings of the workers. Yesterday, except for the five factories in the concession area that fully resumed work, only two factories in Zhabei District started work, and the rest stopped work uniformly. The labor and management have negotiated on the method, and it is difficult to predict whether they will start work this morning.

Labor and Management Consultation

The Six District Sericulture Industry Trade Union has been repeatedly misunderstood by the workers, causing repeated twists and turns. The factory has taken the opportunity to temporarily stop the car. If this is delayed, it will inevitably affect the livelihood of the workers. Therefore, in order to seek a quick solution, yesterday, the board members Yang Gengdi, Yuan Yunlong, Wu Suzhen, etc., were specially dispatched to the Silk Industry Trade Union to discuss the methods with Chairman Shen Huachen, requesting that each factory be notified to start work as usual, so as to avoid additional complications. Shen Junyun immediately persuaded each factory to start the car as usual, and the trade union earnestly persuaded the workers to enter the factory to work, so as not to cause further twists and turns and increase the losses of both parties.

Resumption of Work in the Concession

Taixing, Jingwei, Yuanhetaiji, Xiangyuan on Gansu Road, and Yuyuan on Guoqing Road, the five silk factories on Alabashito Road in the concession area, were also affected by the workers' strike in Zhabei District. At the time, the factories gathered to discuss and decided that the production system issue should be submitted to the authorities for handling, and explained to the workers, so the Jingwei and Xiangyuan factories had already resumed work the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, the other three factories also completed the repair of engines, furnaces, and other machines, and started work as usual. All the workers have also entered the factory to work, and the order is very good.

Situation in Zhabei

The Chu Xin, Hong Tai, Yuan Xing, and other 21 silk factories along Changan Road, Guangfu Road, and Xin Zhabei Meiyuan Road in Zhabei District did not start the car yesterday morning and postponed the start. Only the Xie Xing on Changan Road and the Ruilun on Guangfu Road were not affected and worked as usual. The other 19 factories were shut down.

Page 12

Notice to Start the Car

The Silk Industry Trade Union, at the request of the Six District Sericulture Trade Union, notified the 19 silk factories including Xie Xing separately yesterday, so that the workers could enter the factory to resume work from this morning.

Trade Union's Opinion

According to Dagong News Agency, the union said that the workers originally intended to resume work uniformly the day before yesterday, but because each factory did not start the car, they could not resume work. Although the labor and management have now negotiated and decided to persuade them to start the car to work, the opinions of each factory are not unified, and half of them lack raw materials. The persons in charge have gone to Wuxi and Yixing to collect cocoons. It is difficult to predict whether each factory can start the car uniformly. However, the workers are simple-minded. As long as one or two factories do not start the car, it will inevitably affect each factory, so I hope that each factory will also understand the workers' difficulties and not cause additional complications, so as not to cause new disputes.

Chamber of Commerce's Statement

According to Xinsheng News Agency, Shen Huachen, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, told the reporter of Xinsheng News Agency yesterday that the workers' strike was initially due to the implementation of the production system in each factory, which has been resolved by the government. Now, after the workers' resumption of work, they have been repeatedly misunderstood and evolved into a repeated strike. It is the instigation of the disruptors. The Chamber of Commerce has decided to go to the Social Affairs Bureau within the day to request the party and government agencies to issue a joint notice to set a date for the resumption of work, and to notify the Public Security Bureau to strictly suppress the disruptors and send police to protect the resumption of work.

China Production and Sales Joint Company: Developing a National Goods Plan 113

Cooperation in Production and Promotion

Cooperation in Economy and Talent

The China National Goods Production and Sales Joint Company, initiated by Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Wu Zhihao, a leader in the national goods industry, representatives to the Chicago Exposition, and figures from Shanghai's financial and industrial sectors, aims to establish organized development for national goods and defend China's economic barriers. Recently, the preparatory office of the company has drafted a summary of the business plan procedures to be carried out, which is excerpted below:

Conducting Business: The company conducts business with the aim of cultivating the strength of national goods promotion and creating three major lifelines: increasing production and improving exports. The procedures are divided into three major lifelines: (1) Cooperation in production and promotion; (2) Cooperation in production and economy; (3) Cooperation in economy and talent.

Production and Promotion: The work of cooperation in production and promotion must be based on joint factories and the creation of promotional forces. The joint factory is the work that should be focused on during the preparatory stage, and then engage in the work of creating promotional forces. Creating promotional forces is based on two major principles: developing domestic and foreign business of national goods. These principles, according to the description of the same business procedures, are divided into three types: promotion ordering firms, promotion spot firms, and promotion stores, which are implemented step by step according to the situation and needs of the environment. At the same time, contact existing national goods companies. The procedures for carrying out business should be divided into three areas: (1) For those belonging to this port, plan and coordinate with others to establish national goods stores, the so-called chain stores, or spider web-like stores, in order to obtain statistics on the distribution of national goods consumers and statistics on the popularity of national goods, hold regional national goods exhibitions, and invite established national goods companies to coordinate; (2) For those belonging to other ports, plan and coordinate with others to establish promotion ordering or promotion spot firms, first take the residence of the representatives who participated in the Chicago Exposition this time, or the land within their sphere of influence, as a pilot area, and then expand the scope to the chambers of commerce in various places or the backbone figures in various places, and then plan to establish national goods stores or national goods companies, and contact those who have already established national goods companies; (3) For those belonging to foreign countries, the founders currently attending the Chicago Exposition plan to organize national goods promotion firms, first take Chicago as a pilot area, and then gradually expand the scope, and then plan to establish national goods stores or national goods companies. If this promotion network can be used well, its greatest effectiveness will be enough to resist the intrusion of economic forces and build a barrier for the country in economic defense. Even from the perspective of its smallest effectiveness, it is enough to gather the consumer power of the people, thereby attracting economic strength to coordinate with the production sector, increase the quantity of goods, and improve the quality of products.

Production and Economy: The work of cooperation in production and economy must be based on joint financial circles and manufacturing plants. Joint financial circles are the work that should be focused on during the preparatory stage. When this work has been substantially completed, then engage in obtaining accurate statistics on the popularity of factory-made products. Based on the statistics of this popularity, on the one hand, engage in uniting banks that are enthusiastic about cooperating with national goods, and on the other hand, plan to organize financial institutions that assist national goods, in order to assist manufacturing plants, so that they can increase production and improve products. In general, any factory has the heart to increase production and improve products, but it is trapped by economic reasons, which makes the mind and strength contrary. Even bankers have the heart to cooperate with national goods, but they often suffer because of the lack of understanding of the value of national goods, thus reducing their enthusiasm for cooperation. If there is an institution that can make banks believe, and this institution has the great ability to promote national goods, and is willing to guarantee banks' cooperation with national goods, and there are statistics on the accurate popularity of national goods for reference, then no bank will be unwilling to engage in this business. The principle of bank business is to seek stable interest. If its mortgage can ensure that the specified interest is obtained, and the recovery of the mortgage is very stable, then from the perspective of the principle of business, it is in line with the principle and far better than the most practical and stable business of credit lending. The work of uniting banks that are enthusiastic about assisting national goods must be summarized into a stable method according to the above views, arouse the attention of the banking community, and engage in organizing national goods public warehouses. The goods in the warehouse can be directly mortgaged to the bank by the factory introduced by the company. The financial institutions that organize and assist national goods plan to adopt the organization to promote national goods savings associations, or labor-capital mutual aid savings associations. The organization law and effectiveness of promoting national goods savings associations have been detailed in the business plan for building national goods. As for the labor-capital mutual aid savings association, it is a new route to create labor-capital cooperation. It is not only a financial institution that assists national goods. If this organization can be completed, then labor-capital disputes can be resolved immediately, and all workers can become the most powerful soldiers in the production sector. This proposition has been approved by some members of the General Labor Union this year, and those on the factory side who have heard this proposition have also expressed great sympathy. According to the trend of this opinion, the labor-capital mutual aid savings association is not only a financial institution that assists national goods.

Talent and Economy: The work of cooperation between talent and economy is based on uniting talent and cultivating talent. The work of uniting talent must be carried out by category and organize various research institutions, and then there will be continuous contributions to both production and sales, enough to assist the cooperation in production and promotion and the cooperation in production and economy. For example, the improvement of a product must require its person to have a comparative understanding of similar products and have the academic ability and plan to improve it. However, this kind of talent cannot be hired by a factory with weak resources, or barely hired. However, whether it can be given appropriate command to make the most of its strengths is also a question. Other talents with talent and learning suffer from having no place to display themselves, and the organization that needs talent also suffers from having no place to find them, resulting in two incompatible situations, causing intangible losses to the progress of human resources and productivity in our country. Also, if a person with invention ability cannot obtain economic assistance, this ability cannot be realized or developed rapidly, resulting in a worthless abandonment. People with economic strength, although they have the idea of building a career, also cannot meet the right person, so that this idea cannot become a reality. As for cultivating talent, it is an urgent task for our country today. Furthermore, in terms of the quality and spirit of our people's talent, intelligence, diligence, hard work, and courage to struggle, it is indeed like a fertile field suitable for planting, but no one cultivates it. If it is cultivated, its achievements are really immeasurable. This is evident from the shooting performance of the Chinese team in the Shanghai International Business Corps Rifle Competition. If the work of uniting talent and cultivating talent can be carried out in an organized manner, and then cooperated with the economy, then there will be no abandoned talent and no wasted land. If we talk about it to the fullest extent, then with the lack of productivity of our country's land and the superiority of the quality of the people's talent, if we can do our best to use it to reach the realm of self-sufficiency, it is not absolutely impossible. Today's reliance on foreign goods and oppression by the enemy is our country's self-abandonment. Chapter by chapter, section by section, detailed descriptions, such as propaganda agencies and agency agencies, are extremely important. The former is the hub for supporting the progress of various cooperation, and the latter is the source for planning various raw material factories and developing agricultural and mining industries. To the fullest extent, it is a plan to resist economic aggression, cultivate production strength, and unite agriculture, industry, and commerce to fight against foreign countries. If we can proceed step by step, then after a few years, the foreign goods that are active in the market today will lose their opportunity to invade under the strict barriers.

Relieving the Sale of Chinese Tea to Russia 115

Banking Industry Has Agreed to Grant Loans

Dagon News Agency said that the export of Chinese tea is a major commodity of our country. In recent years, due to poor baking and lack of decoration, it has been subjected to dumping and crowding out by Indian and Japanese tea. The business has plummeted, and Chinese tea merchants have suffered heavy losses and have difficulties in turnover. The tea leaves accumulated in this city are huge. The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in view of this, convened a Chinese tea conference to discuss relief methods. When Chinese tea is sold to Russia, it is also a large commodity. However, Russian merchants have never traded in cash when purchasing Chinese tea, and it takes a year to pay the money. On the Chinese tea merchant side, due to the sluggish business and economic difficulties in recent years, they are unable to lend money, so the sale of Chinese tea to Russia has been suspended invisibly, and they dare not easily conclude a deal. The Trade Bureau submitted the above situation to the Ministry of Industry for approval. After the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance discussed it once, it was decided that the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry would send personnel to contact the Shanghai banking industry for loan methods. As a result, it was decided that after the tea merchants from China and Russia conclude a tea sales transaction, the Russian merchants will be given a one-year repayment period. The money will be temporarily paid by the Shanghai banking industry to the Chinese tea merchants. When the one-year period expires, the Russian merchants must repay the bank in full, including principal and interest. Yesterday, Guo Weibai, director of the International Trade Bureau, claimed that the plan had been agreed by the banking industry, and the Russian Merchants Association had also started to handle the goods. If this is carried out, the law is good and the intention is beautiful. On the one hand, it can promote the sale of Chinese tea to Russia, and on the other hand, it can dredge the financing of Chinese tea merchants. Otherwise, Russian merchants will inevitably purchase goods from India and Japan, and the loss of Chinese tea merchants' newly delayed accumulation is even more unimaginable.

The Hydrographic Office yesterday issued two types of shipping announcements: (1) Announcement on the Southeast Coast and Hong Kong Dangerous Goods Ship Anchorages; (A) Cancellation of the (East) Dangerous Goods Ship Anchorage, Orientation, Kellett Island Flagpole, namely East Longitude about 114 degrees 11 minutes, North Latitude about 22 degrees 17 minutes, Description: The broken line marking this anchorage on the map and the record of (East Dangerous Goods Ship Anchorage) should be deleted together. The scope of the anchorage is listed on the left: Starting from 0.4 chains (10 chains combined into 1 nautical mile) due north of Kellett Island, turn 3 chains due north and turn to 265 degrees 2.55 chains due north, resonating from Kellett Island to 180 degrees due north to the coast. (The mountain boundary of the anchorage is connected to the eastern boundary of the Hong Kong anchorage of the British fleet)) (B) Relocation of the (East) Dangerous Goods Ship Anchorage, Orientation, (1) Point East Longitude 114 degrees 12 minutes 36 seconds, North Latitude 22 degrees 18 degrees 18 degrees minutes 36 seconds, (2) Point East 114 degrees 12 minutes 36 seconds, North Latitude 22 degrees 18 minutes 12 seconds, Description: According to the scope of the dangerous goods ship anchorage listed below, draw a broken line on the map, and add (East Dangerous Goods Ship Anchorage) within this scope. The scope of the anchorage is listed on the left: North boundary, from the above-mentioned (1) point to 90 degrees due north, until the seaside, the south boundary line from the above-mentioned (2) point, to 105.5 degrees due north, until the seaside, the west boundary line, a straight line connecting (1) and (2) points; (2) The movement of the lighthouse pile in the sand channel of Haibei Port in the Yangzi River estuary on the east coast, the new orientation, from the (Changfusha) beacon 284 degrees due north, a distance of 2.84 nautical miles, namely East Longitude about 120 degrees, 31 minutes North Latitude about 32 degrees 5 minutes, Description: Because the river bank was washed down by water, the (Haibei Port Sand) lighthouse pile has been moved to the above-mentioned orientation, and its nature remains the same.

Factories Should Establish Factory Meetings 119

Consultative Resolution of All Issues Between Labor and Management

The Municipal Party Department Notified Trade Unions and Factories to Comply The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department yesterday notified all trade unions and factories, saying: For notification purposes, it is found that Chapter 10 of the Factory Law stipulates that factories should establish factory meetings, which are organized by an equal number of representatives from both labor and management, to consult and resolve all issues between labor and management, and to communicate opinions and connect feelings. The law is good and the intention is beautiful, and it should be organized in accordance with the law as a whole, and actively carried out, so that both labor and management can benefit together. In addition to the separate orders, it is also urgently printed and issued the Factory Law and the relevant articles of the Implementation Regulations on Factory Meetings, so that they can be followed and reported. Do not violate them. This order, Standing Committee Members Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Tong Hangbai.

The Bar Association: Approved to Continue Collecting Construction Fees 120

For the Construction of a Meeting Hall

The Shanghai Bar Association purchased a private house at 572 Beile Road, French Concession, in June of the 18th year of the Republic of China, and converted it into an association. Since then, new members who applied to join the association have been required to pay 50 silver dollars each for the construction of the association's foundation. For several years, new members have complied with the regulations. This year, because Cha Nanqiang lawyer opposed this construction fee, he repeatedly submitted a request to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, stating that the above-mentioned donation was not included in the regulations of the Shanghai Bar Association. The Ministry of Justice ordered the Jiangsu Higher Court to order the Shanghai Bar Association to submit a factual report for verification and handling. At that time, when Cha Nanqiang lawyer joined the association, he did not pay this construction fund, and he was allowed to join the association immediately. However, the association believed that future members who joined the association could refuse to pay, so the Standing Committee continued to submit a request to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, saying that it intended to build a meeting hall that could accommodate more than 1,000 people on the current association, and each member who joined the association should pay 50 yuan for the construction fund, requesting the Ministry of Law to file it. The Ministry of Law has now approved and issued an instruction that all new members who request to join the association must still pay 50 yuan for the construction of the association, and it is approved for filing. It has already been instructed to the Shanghai Bar Association to check.

General Assembly of Accountants Association (Continued) 121

(4) Opening Remarks: Chairman Xie Lin said, distinguished guests, representatives of various associations, today is the opening day of the National Accountants Association. I am very grateful for the representatives of various agencies and groups to come to the meeting to guide us. There are currently representatives from eight accountants' trade unions in Shanghai, Tianjin, Nanjing, Zhejiang, Wuhan, Jiujiang, Guangdong, and Shandong. It can be seen that they attach importance to this meeting. Now I will respectfully speak about the past experience of accountants in our country, the relationship with society, and the necessity of organizing this association. The system of accountants originated in Europe and the United States and was introduced to China. In short, it recognizes accounting as a specialized discipline, and regards those who have this discipline as specialists, and makes specialized professions. The knowledge of accounting is usually nothing more than managing accounts. However, whether managing accounts can be done properly is easy to say but difficult to do. In general, a business has a situation, and the organization of its accounting must be different accordingly. Moreover, in this era of fierce competition in industry and commerce, such as the amount of cost, the rise and fall of management, and the surplus or deficit of business, all depend on the accounting system to express it, and the future plan relies on accounting to standardize it. Therefore, the discipline of accounting is not only necessary for the industrial and commercial circles, but even becomes a specialized technology. For example, building a house, in the past, summoning a tile carpenter was enough to do it. Now the construction has progressed, and high-rise buildings are often dozens of stories high. All facilities require academic knowledge, and every brick and every piece of wood has physics, so there are so-called engineers who are born in response to the times. There are also various distinctions among engineers, some specializing in roads, some specializing in bridges, and some specializing in construction. Others, such as physicians who are divided into internal medicine and surgery, and lawyers who are divided into criminal and civil affairs, each have their own expertise, which is also the same situation. Our accountants are also equal to engineers, physicians, and lawyers, and not only engage in ordinary accounting, but also have specialized skills, such as government accounting, factory accounting, bank accounting, railway accounting, cost accounting, and statistics, etc., each of which is a specialty. In October of the 19th year of the Republic of China, Kong Xiangxi, Minister of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government, convened a conference on industry and commerce. The proposals of various provinces to reform industrial and commercial accounting and to conduct industrial and commercial statistics accounted for many, which shows that accounting affairs have been emphasized by the whole country, and it is also the responsibility that the members of our association in various places should bear for the industrial and commercial circles. The accounting system in our country began in the 7th year of the Republic of China. First, the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce of the old Beijing government promulgated the Interim Regulations for Accountants. Until the 19th year, the National Government graduated, or taught as a professor, and served in a major accounting position in a government agency or a company with a capital of more than 100,000 yuan for more than two years, and was qualified by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to obtain an accountant certificate. It is nothing more than the meaning of emphasizing both learning and experience. It is found that there are currently 1,050 approved accountants. There are already public associations established in various provinces, including Shanghai, Tianjin, Nanjing, Zhejiang, Wuhan, Jiujiang, Guangdong, Shandong, etc., with more than 500 members. The duties given to accountants in the regulations are the organization of accounting, the management of accounting, the audit of accounting, the sorting of accounting, the liquidation of accounting, the certification of accounting, and the appraisal of accounting. It is also stipulated that accountants can be inspectors, liquidators, bankruptcy trustees, will executors, other trustees, and litigation events. The court makes judgments based on the accountant's appraisal report, which has become a proper way, which shows the needs of society. Before our country had accountants, when foreign merchants came to China to do business, accounting affairs were handled by accountants from their own countries. Therefore, there are also a lot of foreign accountants in Shanghai. Their original names are either bookkeepers, or auditors, or accounting experts. Companies and banks in our country have entrusted them. Since recent years, there have been more and more accountants opening businesses in our country, so it is no longer necessary to entrust foreign accountants. In addition, the huge relationship between lawsuits involving non-treaty nationals and our country's courts is also great. Today's business is becoming more and more heavy, which shows its huge relationship even more. Today's meeting is an association for the organization of the National Accountants Association. There are two reasons why it is necessary to have this organization: (1) Mutual assistance in business. Because the business of accountants in our country is still in its infancy, and members are scattered in various places, it is really necessary to help each other in performing business. Therefore, this association is organized as a hub for research and discussion, so that the ability of our accountants can be improved, and the industrial and commercial circles can benefit more. (2) Exchange of knowledge. Because our country has a vast territory, accountants serve the society, and the customs and organizations of the industrial and commercial circles in various places are not clear to each other. Not only can it facilitate the business of the same industry, but it can also contribute to the government as a reference for legislation. It is hoped that the public associations and their members in various places will adhere to this main purpose and maintain the purpose of this association. The guests present today are either the supervisors of accountants, or the guiding bodies of social undertakings, or the leaders of the industrial and commercial circles, or the groups of the academic circles. We must understand that the duties of accountants have a close relationship with society. Regardless of whether this meeting is adjourned, please give practical guidance. I cannot express my sincere hope enough. On behalf of the association today, I would like to thank the guests for their presence and congratulate the development of the accountants' associations in various places and the success of this association. (5) Jiang Hao, representative of the Central Party Department, Tao Baichuan, representative of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, Wu Huanru, representative of the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau, Wang Zhinan, representative of the Municipal Security Office, Lin Kanghou, representative of the Banking Branch of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, Qin Runqing, representative of the Money Industry Association, Shen Junru, representative of the Bar Association, Xu Naili, representative of the National Medical Association Federation, and various guests and journalists spoke one after another (the speeches are omitted). Chairman Xi Yushu delivered a thank you speech. (6) Nomination of proposal reviewers, dividing into groups to review proposals, (Legal System Group) Zhao Zuwei, Tang Zaizhang, Bei Zuyi, Xie Lin, Lu Fuzhen, Lang Junwei, Li Ziying, Wen Yiyou, appointed Zhao representative Zuwei as the convener, (Business Group) Jiang Wanping, Qin Kaichen, Ri Ping, He Yuanming, Tao Senjie, Cheng Xianzhe, Xia Sunhuan, Zhang Jiadong, Zhuo Dingmou, appointed Jiang representative Wanping as the convener, (General Affairs Group) Chen Qixiang, Wang Haifan, Yu Huairen, Wang Sifang, Ouyang Hancun, Huang Renqiang, Xi Yushu, Chen Chaolun, Yang Zengxun, appointed Chen representative Qixiang as the convener, (7) Photography, (8) Dinner, (9) Reception of representatives of public associations from various places to participate in the naming ceremony of five aircraft, and it is heard that the first meeting of the Proposal Review Committee is scheduled to be held at 11:00 am on the 11th of this month at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club.

Shanghai North Station Inauguration Ceremony Yesterday 122

=Ministry of Railways Sends Counselor Zhang Weici to Open the Key=

=Director Huang Boqiao Personally Conducts the Flag-Raising Ceremony=

The four-story building of Shanghai North Station of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration was destroyed by Japanese aircraft during the January 28 Incident last year, leaving only the foundation. After the ceasefire, the Railway Administration immediately found another building to serve as a temporary office, and in mid-August, it submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways to rebuild the upper floor. Later, the proposal to relocate the station was put on hold due to the city government's proposal to relocate the station. Later, due to the serious national crisis, the Ministry ordered a temporary suspension of the station relocation, so the old matter was re-examined and construction started in early June. Now it has been fully completed, and an inauguration ceremony was held yesterday afternoon, and guests from all walks of life were invited to visit. The details of the situation are recorded below.

Engineering Notes 123

The location of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration was at the Shanghai North Station. Originally, it was a four-story building, 60.5 meters long and 24.7 meters wide, covering a total area of 1,494.55 square meters. It was divided into 76 rooms and was built according to the blueprints designed by the British engineer, West Repley. The corners of the building on three sides were made of Qingdao granite. The large walls above the first floor were supported by steel columns, and all the wall foundations, column bases, and floors were constructed with foreign cement and aggregate. The building was completed on the 20th day of May in the first year of the Xuantong reign of the late Qing Dynasty. The total cost was 329,448 silver dollars. Not only was it magnificent, but the materials used were also extremely strong. Therefore, after more than 20 years, it still showed no signs of changing its original state. Unexpectedly, it became scorched earth during the January 28th Incident. On January 29th of the 21st year, the second afternoon of the incident, Japanese aircraft circled over the North Station, dropping bombs. The Administration's office building, warehouse, and newly built annex offices were successively hit and caught fire. The raging flames soared into the sky and lasted all night. All books, documents, instruments, and implements were reduced to ashes, with losses amounting to 500,000 yuan. On May 23rd, the North Station area was taken over by this Bureau, and the Engineering Department immediately supervised the demolition of the destroyed station building. Initially, it was planned to demolish only down to the third floor and repair and use the second floor. However, after the rubble on the second floor was cleared, it was observed that the brick and stone work was beyond repair, and it was decided to demolish it completely. As for the ground floor, although there were several places where the brick walls, stone arches, and door and window floors were damaged, they were not seriously affected, so it was planned to repair and use them, and add another floor on top. This proposal was submitted to the Ministry of Railways and approved on August 13th of the 21st year with Directive No. 3884 of the Engineering Department. At that time, the Shanghai Municipal Government proposed relocating the Shanghai North Station in order to promote the prosperity of the Zhabei area and promote the development of the city center. The Railway Ministry instructed the Committee for the Construction of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways to repeatedly send personnel to Shanghai to negotiate. As a result, because the North Station's location was in the center of the Zhabei District, and there was no room for future development of the two railway lines, and it was especially important to the overall plan of the Shanghai city center, it was decided to accept the Shanghai Municipal Government's suggestion and select a site south of Dava Road and north of Xiangyin Road, along the southwest 1,800 meters of Zhongshan Road, as the location for the passenger terminal. A site west of Zhongshan Road and east of Zhenru Road, along the existing railway line, would be used as the intermodal terminal. The proposal to rebuild the Shanghai North Station was thus shelved. In March of the 22nd year, the Ministry of Railways, due to the seriousness of the national crisis, ordered the cessation of the station relocation. The Bureau, mindful that the Shanghai North Station was a matter of concern for both Chinese and foreigners, felt that it was inappropriate to leave this ruin standing for a long time, giving travelers a bad impression. Moreover, because passengers lacked a place to wait and rest, they usually crowded under the awnings around the ticket office, and

felt very pained. Therefore, it was decided to repair the lower floor of the building and rebuild a central part of the upper floor, so that the Traffic Department could move in to work, and passengers could have a place to wait and rest. This was submitted to the Ministry of Railways and approved on April 14th of the 22nd year with Directive No. 11506 of the T Department. Subsequently, the architect Zhao Shen of the Huayi Architectural Firm was entrusted to revise the original plan of the Engineering Department and provide drawings. The Engineering Department then invited bids for the project. At 3:00 PM on May 1st, the bidding was opened publicly in the Bureau. Commissioner Huang Hongdao was dispatched by the Ministry of Railways to supervise. A total of 17 companies submitted bids. The lowest bid was from the Tao Hongtai Construction Company, with a bid of 47,750 yuan in national currency. The next lowest was from the Qiao Yu and Construction Company, with a bid of 49,850 yuan in national currency. The next lowest was from the Zhongnan Construction Company, with a bid of 50,146 yuan in national currency. It was considered that although this project was not very large, it was a public place, and extra attention had to be paid to its appearance and safety. Therefore, the qualifications and experience of the construction companies had to be carefully considered. Among the companies with lower bids, the Zhongnan Construction Company had undertaken major construction projects for the Shanghai Municipal Engineering Bureau, the Bank of China, and others over the years, with each project reaching 100,000 to 200,000 yuan, and had owner satisfaction certificates, which was most suitable. Moreover, the price difference was not too large. Therefore, after consulting with the Commissioner dispatched by the Ministry to supervise the opening of bids, it was decided to award the project to the company. The contract was formally signed on May 17th. The supervision and guidance of the construction work was entrusted to architect Zhao Shen, and the Ministry of Railways was notified for approval and record. The renovated Shanghai North Station building would mostly be used for the Traffic Department's offices. The center of the hall would house an information desk and reception area, with an electric standard clock above it. The rest would be used for first and second-class passenger waiting rooms, luggage storage rooms, and restaurants. Negotiations were held with the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications to install six public telephones in the south of the hall (which could also be used for long-distance calls). A model book stall would be set up in the southwest corner, and other stations would be handled in the same way in the future. At the same time, the surroundings of the station would be rearranged to create a clean and beautiful environment. The building construction started on May 17th. It was delayed by rain in the middle, and the entire project was completed on August 25th. Commissioner Huang Hongdao of the Ministry of Railways was dispatched on August 31st to inspect and accept the project, together with Mo Heng, the Chief of the General Affairs Department of the Bureau, and Desford, the Chief of the Engineering Department. Although it was not possible to fully restore the old appearance, it was a great improvement compared to the devastated scene after the fire.

Guest Visitors 124

The following people visited the station yesterday: Minister of Communications Zhu Jia驊, Director of the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways Yu Yan, President of Jiaotong University Li Zhaobao, Acting Garrison Commander of Songhu Zhang Xiang, Director of the Central Mint Lu Xuepu, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government Yu Hongjun, Director of the Security Department Yang Hu, Guo Shun, Ren Chuanbang, Hu Pu'an, and about a hundred reporters from Chinese and foreign newspapers.

Completion Ceremony 125

The completion and key-opening ceremony was held at 2:00 PM. First, the municipal military band played music. The Director of the Two Railways Bureau, Huang Boqiao, personally performed the flag-raising ceremony. Then, Counselor Zhang Weici of the Ministry of Railways opened the lock. The simple and solemn ceremony came to an end. Director Huang and all the staff led guests from all walks of life into the station to visit the offices on each floor and explain everything. After walking around for a week, they returned to the ground floor for refreshments and dispersed.

Hopes of the Authorities 126

Huang Boqiao, Director of the Two Railways Bureau, and Wu Shaozeng, Deputy Director, expressed their hopes for the completion of the restored Shanghai North Station, saying that the reconstruction of the Shanghai North Station was the result of the January 28th Incident, and the January 28th Incident was the result of the September 18th Incident. Therefore, today's reception for all sectors to visit the completed reconstruction of the Shanghai North Station does not mean we are celebrating. However, there are a few points that I would like to take this opportunity to report, hoping that everyone will have a certain understanding after visiting the site, and then give us guidance and assistance. First, what we want to report is that the railway is mainly based on business, and the state-owned railway is mainly based on commercialization. According to the current organization of the Railway Bureau, the center of business operation is in the Traffic Department. Therefore, we still set up the Traffic Department in the Shanghai North Station, the center of the two railways. The Traffic Department has recently revised its organization, reorganized the Document Section into the General Affairs Section, the Dispatch Section into the Transportation Section, and the Commercial Section into the Business Section. Under this Business Section, there are also the Document Stock, Passenger Transport Stock, Freight Stock, Compilation and Investigation Stock, Public Relations Stock, and Catering Stock. At the same time, starting today, the Business Office recently established at 407 Jing'an Temple Road in Shanghai, also belongs to the Business Section of the Traffic Department, and is almost a branch office. In the near future, we also want to have the same setup in the southern part of Shanghai. We want to thoroughly realize the commercialization of state-owned railways consistently inside and out. Second, what we want to report is that the railway serves the people, and should mainly provide the public with full convenience and safety. Therefore, in addition to trains, we also strive to rectify the equipment at the stations. We will first designate several large stations as model stations to refresh them. The Shanghai North Station is the center of the two railways, and Shanghai, where it is located, occupies the most important position in our country's economy. There are about 300,000 passengers traveling to and from each month.

However, since the station building was burned down, passengers have long lacked a place to wait, and third and fourth-class passengers lack adequate waiting facilities. Now that we have restored the Shanghai North Station, we have divided a part of the ground floor for first and second-class passengers, and used awnings with windows at the back of the station building to set up seats and add new-style men's and women's restrooms for third and fourth-class passengers. We have also set up a special luggage storage area, so that passengers who only have a short stay in Shanghai can temporarily deposit their luggage without having to carry it with them to avoid burdens. We have a special agreement with the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications to install public telephones, which can also be used for long-distance calls. In addition, wired and wireless telegraphs and postal services are planned to be added to the station in succession after consultation with the transportation authorities for direct delivery. In addition, the North Station is an important station for the two railways, and the passengers and vehicles entering and leaving the station are the most crowded. If there is no proper management method, the order will be chaotic. Therefore, this time we restored the Shanghai North Station, and at the same time, we will thoroughly rectify the traffic inside and outside the station. As far as the inside of the station is concerned, in the past, the routes for passengers and luggage carts were mixed and not separated. Now, they are separately stipulated to make them orderly. Outside the station, we have also demarcated parking areas for automobiles and rickshaws, and deployed police posts along the routes so that passengers and vehicles can travel according to their destinations without colliding and causing danger. In addition, there are no public restaurants in the stations of the two railways. This time, the North Station will be restored, and it is planned to run it immediately so that passengers traveling to and from can get economical and clean food at any time. In addition, the expansion of the rain shed platform at Nanjing Xiaguan Station and the repair of other major stations will also be completed at the same time. Third, what we want to report is that railway transportation is based on speed and reliability. Therefore, what we are most committed to is to make the train arrive on time at the prescribed time. Once this is done, we will then seek to shorten the driving time within the prescribed time. Part of the train schedule changed on June 1 of this year was to achieve this goal. For example, the Beijing-Shanghai daytime express train was shortened from the longest eight hours and fifteen minutes to six hours and fifty minutes. Freight trains have been changed from indefinite departures to eight times a day. The Shanghai-Hangzhou freight trains have also been changed from once every other day to every day. Now we are retesting the traction of locomotives, and from September 1st, we will shorten the running time of various trains again. For example, the first and second passenger trains and the Beijing-Zhabei express trains will be reduced by 30 minutes (from Beijing to Shanghai, it now only takes six hours and twenty minutes), the fifth Beijing-Shanghai night express train will be reduced by 30 minutes, and the 11th and 12th Shanghai-Beijing third and fourth-class slow trains will have their running time reduced by one hour and fifteen minutes and two hours respectively. The 301st and 302nd domestic intermodal express trains will be reduced by half an hour and 35 minutes respectively. The shortening of freight trains is even greater. For example, the 311th Beijing-Shanghai freight train will be reduced by 15 hours and eight minutes compared to before, and the 312th freight train will be reduced by 17 hours and twelve minutes (the shortest time for freight trains from Beijing to Shanghai used to be 19 hours and 37 minutes, and now the shortest is only 16 hours and 25 minutes). In addition, mixed passenger and freight trains have been added, so that sporadic freight cars or loaded cars that have not been taken away by freight trains can be transported at any time along the way, which is especially fast. But we are not satisfied with this. In the future, we will continue to shorten the time as much as possible within the possible range. To summarize the three points reported above, our only purpose is to use a reasonable method with twelve points of determination to operate the railway and fulfill the mission of serving the people. However, those in charge are confused, and onlookers are clear. Therefore, we want to take the opportunity of repairing the Shanghai North Station to invite leaders from all walks of life to see a part of our facilities on the spot and listen to our brief report. After that, they will give us instructions and assistance anytime and anywhere, so that we can improve what we have not done well and make up for what we have not done. This is what we desperately desire.

False Trademarks of Lei Yunshang, Continued Arrest of Criminals Escorted to Shanghai 128

=Haimen Huaize Hall Pharmacy Owner=

=Wang Hazhang has been prosecuted in the case=

On the 25th of last month, the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, at Yutai Medicinal Material Store at 151 Xiangguajie outside Xiaodongmen in Nanshi, and Lida Pharmacy at 1 Hengxing Xili on the opposite side of the road, were found to have set up a wholesale agency for counterfeit secret Liu Shen Wan and American Ginseng medicines of the Lei Yunshang Songfen Hall Pharmacy, and arrested Yang Zhengming, Gui Hanjiang, Tan Youcai, Ji Ruiding, and other four people. On the spot, they seized a lot of the above-mentioned counterfeit drugs, and evidence of the imitation, and brought them back to the team for interrogation. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. It is now known that Gui Hanjiang also confessed that his accomplice, Wang Hazhang from Haimen, also falsely produced Lei Yunshang's military powder, Biewen Pills, Sha medicine, toad cake pills, and other medicines, and sold them in the Huaize Hall Pharmacy in Haimen. After the leader of the Lu team according to the confession, he ordered the detective team leader Chen Caifu to lead the detectives Mao Gongzhao, Zeng Wanli, and Li Guiting, and others, to take documents to the Haimen Public Security Bureau the other day, added police, and went to the Huaize Hall Pharmacy in Changxing Town, Haimen, arrested the shop owner Ningbo native Wang Hazhang, and copied out the Biewen Pills, military powder, Sha medicine, toad cake pills, imitation medicine bottles, and escorted them by ship to Shanghai yesterday morning. According to Wang Hazhang's confession, he is 68 years old, from Ningbo, lived in Changxing Town, Haimen, and opened the Huaize Hall Pharmacy. Four years ago, the military powder Sha medicine toad cake pills and other medicine of Lei Yunshang was filled with Jiangbei, which greatly affected the business of our brand's medicine. For the sake of livelihood, I had no choice but to inquire around, and then learned that there were various medicine bottles and imitation medicine bottles made of Lei Yunshang in Jiangbei, and used my brand's medicines at home to store and sell, in order to maintain life. This matter has only been a year or so, but Lei Yunshang wants to ban counterfeit products, and must fundamentally solve it. First, the Jiangxi kiln must be banned from burning counterfeit magnetic bottles, and Jiangbei must be informed of the investigation and ban. For the sake of morality, it is not convenient for those who sell Lei Yunshang's medicine bottles and imitation medicine bottles.

to be exposed. If Lei Yunshang is lenient to me, I am willing to help him ban it in various stores in Jiangbei. After the leader of the Lu team verified the confession, he said that Wang's violation of the trademark was the same in everything, and should be prepared to be sent to the bureau for legal action.

Young Explorer Chen Yiqin Returns to Hong Kong 129

=The first phase of exploration work is completed=

Street Love Talk 130

Because of conflict, he angered the police officer, and the preliminary hearing said that the behavior was improper. At about 9:00 p.m. the night before, in the Lukiazai area of Guangqi Road in the city, a well-dressed young man suddenly put his arm around the neck of a modern woman, talking and walking there, looking very happy. The woman was wearing a fashionable long cheongsam with blue flowers and a white background, flesh-colored stockings, and high-heeled leather shoes. She was still beautiful, and was caught by the watchman Zhang Huatang of the tenth post in the area. Because their indecent behavior was detrimental to public morals, he immediately stepped forward to stop them. Unexpectedly, the young man raised his voice to the police and said, "She (referring to the woman) is my wife. We love each other. What's it to you?" Officer Zhang then scolded, "Even if you two are indeed a formal couple, you should not be hugging on the road." However, the young man still refused to accept it, so that the two sides suddenly conflicted during the conversation. For a time, a large crowd gathered to watch. At that time, a person suddenly came out and stated that they were not a formal couple, and the modern woman was not a lady from a big family, but actually the eldest sister (female servant) of a certain family on Guangqi Road. When the woman saw that their secret was revealed, her cheeks turned red in an instant. The onlookers laughed at the sight. Officer Zhang immediately ordered the person to act as a witness temporarily, and detained both the man and the woman and brought them in. The third office of the first district under its jurisdiction was preliminarily examined by the chief of the Liu office, first confirming that the witness was Zhu Xilin, 23 years old, from Wuxi. The woman was indeed a female servant of a certain family. However, I do not know the young man." Questioning the young man, he said that his name was Xu Bingwen, 23 years old, from Wuxi, and he heard that he was a partner in a cotton cloth shop on a certain major road in the British Concession. This woman is really my fiancee, etc. Questioning the woman, she said that her name was Xu Yongzhen, 16 years old, from Zhenjiang, and is currently a servant in a certain family at No. 4 Guangqi Road. The rest of the words were vague. Because their behavior was improper, they were ordered to be fined six yuan each as a warning. At this point, this interesting scene came to an end.

Lamb's Speech: Gandhi's Personality and His Movement 131

The YMCA of the Eight Immortals Bridge specially invited Mr. Lamb, the Secretary-General of the National Association of Indian Christian Youth, to give a speech on "Gandhi's Personality and His Movement" at 4:00 p.m. yesterday. Shen Tishang, the principal of the Mylon Middle School, translated, and Cai Zhaolu of the Bingxun Stenography Agency took shorthand notes. A very large number of people attended the lecture. The following is an excerpt of his speech:

It is said that Gandhi's movement problem is the most important problem in India at present. Because in the history of India, no one has been as believed and worshiped by the people as Gandhi. He pays attention to supporting the motherland and hopes that the world will be loyal and patriotic, just like Gandhi loves his motherland. Gandhi received higher education and studied law in London. After returning to China, he went to South Africa to fight for the unequal treatment of Indians in South Africa and relieve the pain of Indians. Since then, Indians have recognized Gandhi as a leader, and Gandhi himself recognizes that he has an obligation to fight together with his oppressed compatriots. There are three major forces in his struggle, (1. The Bible,) 2. (The Hindu Scriptures,) 3. (Tolstoy's philosophy.) In this struggle, he invented a basic principle, which is the secret of his success, that is, to adhere to the truth forever and unremittingly. Many people say that resistance cannot be translated into truth, but from Gandhi's character, we know that truth and passive resistance are completely different and cannot represent his mission. Passive resistance is the tool of the weak, and upholding the truth is the principle of the strong. Because passive resistance contains a provision for disobeying the law, and the bad consequences of disobeying the law can only be endured, so passive resistance is a last resort. For example, the British women's movement and the Soviet Russian Tolstoy movement represent this mission. This upholding the truth is the strong using civilized forces to resist the brutal barbaric forces, and it contains a kind of doctrine, no matter what, not taking a means of revenge. This movement is a psychological attitude, which is to recognize that the force used is barbaric, and generate power from the suffering. This power can deceive the other party's barbarism, so it is also a non-violent movement. This non-violent movement is not only a political movement, but also a religious movement. Gandhi's use of the non-violent movement has been successful in India many times. Later, the British government passed a special decree, giving local officials and police the power to arbitrarily arrest people without going through legal procedures or interrogation. Gandhi felt that his movement had no hope in politics, so he advocated three points, (1) resisting foreign cloth and promoting native cloth, (2) raising the status of untouchables, (3) political non-cooperation. However, Gandhi's non-violent movement was too slow to succeed, so it was divided into factions. There are some people who advocate assassinating government officials, and some are willing to serve in the government, but always oppose the government. Now that Gandhi has been arrested and imprisoned, everything seems to be stagnant, but compared with 1900, the nation's self-confidence, the nation's spirit of self-determination, and the spirit of struggling for the country and the nation are very swollen. There are three elements to Gandhi's greatness, (1) worshiping the truth, (2) patriotic enthusiasm, sacrificing everything for the patriotic spirit, (3) deeply believing in the spiritual elements, not relying on material things to save individuals and countries.
