The Warden of Civilian Housing, Wang Zhenchang, is Subject to Disciplinary Action 135

=Due to Evidence of Self-Interest and Abuse of Power=

=Salary Reduction of 20% for a Period of Ten Months=

The Shanghai Municipal Civil Service Disciplinary Committee issued a resolution on the disciplinary action against Wang Zhenchang, stating: The person subject to disciplinary action, Wang Zhenchang, the General Warden of Civilian Housing in Shanghai, is 34 years old, a native of Jiaxing, Zhejiang, and resides at the Third Civilian Housing Unit, Jiaotong Road, Zhabei. The aforementioned person subject to disciplinary action was impeached by the Control Yuan for cases of self-interest and abuse of power, and the case was referred to the Judicial Yuan for review. The decision of this committee is as follows: (Ruling) Wang Zhenchang's monthly salary is reduced by 20% for a period of ten months. (Facts) The person subject to disciplinary action, Wang Zhenchang, is the General Warden of Civilian Housing in Shanghai. In May of this year, Xu Haiqing, Xun Jipei, Xu Shaoqing, Han Dexiang, and others successively filed complaints with the Control Yuan, alleging corruption, dereliction of duty, self-interest, abuse of power, and oppression of civilians. The Control Yuan ordered the dispatch of a special investigator, who reported back, stating in brief: It was found that (1) Xu Haiqing of the First Civilian Housing Unit, because his rented No. 6 boiled water shop was connected to No. 21, rented by Yan Bishi, agreed with Yan Bibao of No. 21 to exchange his original rented No. 30 and No. 49. The person subject to disciplinary action had initially approved it, but because he wanted Xu Haiqing to sell the boiled water shop to his relative for 160 yuan and demanded a transfer fee of 40 yuan, he used his power to request a forced eviction, followed by arrest and detention. (2) Xun Jipei and Xu Shaoqing of the Third Civilian Housing Unit, having obtained a license from the Social Bureau to open a boiled water shop, were denied permission to operate by the person subject to disciplinary action because he failed to extort a bribe of 200 yuan. He then, under the guise of a cooperative, requested the revocation of their license. (3) Han Dexiang of the Third Civilian Housing Unit, for convening a meeting to demand rent reduction, was labeled a reactionary by the person subject to disciplinary action and reported to the Public Security Bureau, who arrested and detained him at the local court, eventually released after the court ruled for non-prosecution. It is undeniable that the person subject to disciplinary action acted arbitrarily and oppressed civilians. The Control Committee deemed that the person subject to disciplinary action had violated the law and derelicted his duties, filing an impeachment, and referred it to the Judicial Yuan for disciplinary action. (Reasons) This case is explained in three parts below: (1) Regarding Xu Haiqing: After the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the person subject to disciplinary action left the civilian housing. In May, Xu Haiqing exchanged his originally rented No. 30 and No. 49 houses in the First Civilian Housing Unit with Yan Bibao's originally rented No. 21 house. The person subject to disciplinary action only took office in June of the same year. Xu Haiqing's claim that he had obtained prior permission lacks substantial proof. The investigation form he submitted was issued in December of last year, after the Social Bureau approved the return to the original numbers in August of last year, and was only used for investigating the actual residents at the time, and cannot be used as evidence of prior permission for the exchange. Xu Haiqing's original accusation is not credible. Regarding the accusation of demanding a transfer fee of 40 yuan, Xu Haiqing submitted reports to the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Social Bureau in December of last year and January of this year, stating only that the person subject to disciplinary action, relying on Lü Dianqin and Sun Yunpeng, failed to purchase the boiled water shop from the merchants, hence this eviction strategy, without mentioning any bribery of 40 yuan. Furthermore, this matter was investigated by the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor at Xu Haiqing's request, who deemed that there was insufficient suspicion of a crime and ruled for non-prosecution. This point should be dismissed. However, in June of last year, the person subject to disciplinary action negotiated with Xu Haiqing to sell the boiled water shop to his relative for 160 yuan, which Xu Haiqing did not agree to. Witnesses Lü Dianqin and Sun Yunpeng testified at the meeting, vividly describing the events at the time, which cannot be considered inadmissible. Xu Haiqing, because the person subject to disciplinary action first ordered him to return to the original number, submitted a request to the Social Bureau on July 26 to stop the forced eviction. The Social Bureau issued an order to the person subject to disciplinary action, stating: "Once a resident rents a house, it must not be altered privately. If there is a valid reason and both parties agree to the exchange, it is permissible, but the procedures must be followed. The request must be submitted to the General Warden for review and approval." After receiving the order, the person subject to disciplinary action disregarded the reasons for the mutual convenience of the exchange stated by Xu Haiqing and Yan Bibao, and still ordered them to return to the original numbers, causing Xu Haiqing to submit another request to the Social Bureau, which rejected the limited eviction. The person subject to disciplinary action then submitted a request to the Social Bureau, which forwarded it to the Public Security Bureau for forced eviction, resulting in the arrest of Xu Haiqing and his wife. It is undeniable that he abused his power to oppress residents because his self-interest was not fulfilled. (2) Regarding Xun Jipei and Xu Shaoqing: Xun Jipei and Xu Shaoqing submitted a request to the Social Bureau in October of the 20th year of the Republic, stating that they intended to jointly open a boiled water shop at No. 116 of the Third Civilian Housing Unit and had obtained a registration certificate, but the person subject to disciplinary action did not allow them to open for business. The Social Bureau dispatched personnel to investigate and found that No. 116 of the Third Civilian Housing Unit was rented to Han Naimao. Xun Jipei applied for the registration certificate on July 30 of the 20th year of the Republic, when the house was not yet completed and the house number had not yet been assigned. Xu Shaoqing only rented No. 32 of the housing unit on September 18 of the 20th year of the Republic, which does not match the house number in Xun Jipei's registration certificate. Therefore, Xun Jipei was ordered to surrender the registration certificate, which was not due to the request of the person subject to disciplinary action. The person subject to disciplinary action was not aware of Xun Jipei's application for registration. Although a request was submitted in September of the 20th year of the Republic that the boiled water shop in the Third Civilian Housing Unit be operated by a consumer cooperative, it was unrelated to the reason for Xun Jipei's surrender of the registration certificate. The allegation by Xun Jipei and others that they were extorted for 200 yuan is based on the fact that the person subject to disciplinary action had written a draft agreement and ordered them to copy and sign it, with Article 2 stating that if merchants can subsidize the cooperative by 200 yuan, all boiled water shops and tea shops will be operated by the merchants. The person subject to disciplinary action argued that he did not provide the draft agreement. There is no other way to prove that it was indeed provided by the person subject to disciplinary action. Furthermore, this matter was investigated by the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor at Xun Jipei's request, who deemed that there was no fraud and ruled for non-prosecution. This part should also be dismissed. (3) Regarding Han Dexiang: Han Dexiang distributed an urgent notice in the Third Civilian Housing Unit on May 3 of this year, convening a meeting to demand rent reduction. The person subject to disciplinary action sent it to the Public Security Bureau for review. The Public Security Bureau forwarded it to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor, who deemed that it did not meet the requirements of the crime of disturbing public order under the Criminal Law and did not prosecute. It is not objectionable that the person subject to disciplinary action sent Han Dexiang to the Public Security Bureau for review in order to prevent incidents from occurring. However, in the report submitted to the Social Bureau, it was stated that Han Dexiang was instigated by the communists to incite unrest and disrupt order, without any basis. Such wording, considering the duty of public officials to act cautiously, cannot be said to be anything but rash. In conclusion, except for the dismissed parts, the person subject to disciplinary action has committed acts described in Article 2, Paragraph 1, and Paragraph 2 of the Civil Service Disciplinary Law. In accordance with Article 3, Paragraph 1, Item 3 and Article 6 of the same law, it is resolved as stated in the main text. September 6, 22nd year of the Republic of China, Shanghai Municipal Civil Service Disciplinary Committee, Chairman Zhu Fengwei, Committee Member Zhao Shulan, Committee Member Yao Fuxiang, Committee Member Qian Chengjun, Committee Member Pang Shurong, Committee Member Luo Renji.

The Corpses' Families of the Xin Renhe Tragedy Petition for Provisional Attachment of the Guarantee Money 136

The Xin Renhe steamboat of the Yuxing Shipping Company in the Nanshi district had a tragic incident in which Ma Koubao, Mei Laoer, and three others were murdered. Afterward, the Shanghai Local Court arrested and sentenced the shipowner, Sun Xingsheng, the compradore, Chen Baosheng, and the stewards and sailors. Sun and others refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Suzhou High Court, awaiting interrogation in Suzhou. It has now been learned that the families of the deceased, such as Ma Chenshi, Mei Youshi, Ma Zhoushi, Wei Zhushi, etc., recently hired lawyer Yu Xiangqin to draft a petition to the Local Court Mediation Office, requesting that all of the guarantee money and the pledge money deposited by the 74 defendants, including Sun Xingsheng, be provisionally attached to the Yuxing Company, in order to prevent concealment and facilitate execution. The petition stated, in brief, that according to the general practice of various shipping companies and the confession of the defendant Ye Yuanfu on April 28 of this year, there is no doubt that the incidental civil lawsuit part of the petitioners has been judged by the court that the defendants are jointly and severally liable for compensation, but the defendants cunningly claim that they have no property at home, and they intend to avoid compensation. If this guarantee money and the pledge money are not attached today, it is feared that they will collude to conceal it in the future, making execution difficult. Therefore, the petition requests provisional attachment to prevent concealment and facilitate execution. Furthermore, the petitioners have suffered this extraordinary disaster, and their situation is extremely tragic. They are wandering in a foreign land, facing the danger of freezing and starvation, etc. Judge Han Zuoti held a court session (none of the defendants attended), and only the petitioners' lawyer Yu Xiangqin attended the court and recounted the previous events. The judge said, "Upon investigation, there is no solid proof of the objects of the provisional attachment in this case, and it cannot proceed." Lawyer Yu replied, "The defendant Ye Yuanfu confessed that each steward and sailor had a guarantee money of 500 yuan deposited in the shipping company. Please, Your Honor, exercise your authority to investigate the Yuxing Shipping Company's books, which should make it clear." The judge also said, "The entire case file of the Criminal Court has now been sent to the High Court and cannot be examined." As a result, it was decided to wait for further hearing.

No More Planting is Allowed on the New Prison Site of the Second Branch of the High Court 137

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court recently requisitioned several acres of land in the Pu Song District in western Shanghai to build a prison. When the land was requisitioned, there were still various types of plants growing on it. Now that it is autumn harvest time, the plants can be gradually harvested. The court is deeply concerned that the original owners might continue planting, seeing that the construction has not yet started. Therefore, the president of the court, Shen Jia Yi, issued a prohibition yesterday and had the notice written on a wooden sign, which was placed in the fields. The notice reads as follows: Public Notice: This court is building a new prison in the 30th Bao and 7th Tu of the Pu Song District in this city. The requisitioned land has been fenced off, and a notice has been issued prohibiting infringement. It is understood that the plants planted on this land before the requisition should be allowed for the original owners to harvest at the appropriate time. However, once harvested, no further planting is allowed. If anyone plants on the above-mentioned land or engages in other infringing acts in the future, the Tu Dibao shall be responsible for prohibiting them at any time and for removing the planted plants. If they refuse to comply, they shall be handed over to the police precinct for punishment. All must comply with this notice.

Residents of Yufu Lane in the French Concession Object to the Demolition of Houses 138

An Emergency Meeting Was Held Yesterday. The landlord of the houses in Yufu Lane, Nanyang Bridge, French Concession, notified the tenants in August of this year that the houses would be demolished and rebuilt on September 11, and all tenants were required to move out. The tenants, however, argued that the houses inside the lane were built in 1919, only 14 years ago. The houses are brand new and quite sturdy, and the houses on the outside of the lane were only built 18 years ago, which is not yet the time for rebuilding. Therefore, they unanimously expressed their opposition. They also organized a delegation to request the landlord to maintain the houses for at least another five years. However, the landlord stated that all engineering plans had been completed and that it was difficult to accept the tenants' demands. Starting yesterday, they suddenly cut off the street lights in the lane, plunging the entire lane into darkness. At the same time, they sent people to notify each household that if they did not move out, the water and electricity supply to the tenants would be cut off. Upon hearing this, the tenants were all alarmed and held an emergency meeting at the Fourth District Branch of the Municipal Federation at 4 p.m. yesterday. All the tenants were present, and Yang Yingzhai chaired the meeting. The following resolutions were passed: (1) All tenants will unite to the end and will not move out in the face of any oppression. (2) Yang Yingzhai, Yang Youbin, Jiang Shunjian, and others are designated as representatives to immediately send letters of petition to the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession and the Shanghai Second Special District Municipal Union, seeking help. (3) Another date will be set for all tenants to hold a large-scale petition to the Party and government authorities. (4) If the landlord implements the suspension of water and electricity supply, which will affect public safety and tranquility, they will resolutely file a lawsuit in accordance with the law and declare that the landlord shall be responsible for the resulting losses. (5) Lawyers will be hired to ensure legal protection. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

A Sandboat Was Lost in a Hurricane 139

=All Thirty-Plus People Aboard Survived Except for Four=

=Haizhou Saved Them; What Happened to the Rest is Unknown=

The Hongchangxing sandboat, owned by Tongzhou Liji, was hired by Xiangchengyong Yuji and other firms from Yingkou to sail to Chongsha to transport cotton cloth and other goods worth over 60,000 yuan. After loading the cargo, the boat set sail, but on the first of this month, when it reached the northern sea off Qidong, a strong wind suddenly arose. The waves were rough, but the boat was still able to navigate. However, when it reached the sea off Dajishan, the wind became even stronger. The sailors knew it was a hurricane and tried to seek shelter, but the hurricane became more intense, and the waves crashed over the boat. The boat owner, Mr. Peng, tried to find a port to dock, but the strong wind made it impossible. The sailors were panicking when a gust of hurricane blew, and a large wave crashed down, snapping the mainmast. At this point, the sailors knew that the broken mast meant they had lost the ability to navigate. They were terrified. The thirty-plus people on board called for help to no avail and could only drift with the wind and waves. On the morning of the third, the wind and waves finally pushed them to the northeast coast of Dajishan, where they were stranded on the rocks and overturned. The boat was flooded by the waves. At that time, the sailors saw that the boat was completely flooded and beyond saving. They threw the planks into the sea, clung to them, and waited to be rescued. Five of the sailors drifted on the sea for two days and nights. On the fifth, a Haizhou steamboat passed by, saw them, stopped, lowered the gangplank, and rescued the five sailors. They were given clothes to change and two yuan each, and sent to Haimen to go ashore. One of the sailors died of illness in Haimen. Yesterday, the four rescued sailors came to Shanghai by boat and reported the names of the firms. They said that when the hurricane struck and the waves crashed over the boat, three or four people were washed away. In the panic, they could not remember clearly. After the boat overturned, they desperately tried to save themselves and escaped. The five of them clung to a plank and drifted on the sea waiting to be rescued. Fortunately, the Haizhou steamboat rescued them. The boat owner, Mr. Peng, and the other twenty-seven sailors were not seen on the sea. It is feared that they did not survive. Although the boat is stranded on the rocks, the strong hurricane and waves will surely damage it and wash it away. It will be difficult to go there to find it.

A Bullet at the South Railway Station 140

A Careless Police Officer Luckily Didn't Injure Anyone. At the Shanghai South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, at around 9 a.m. yesterday, the station was preparing to open the third and fourth-class passenger cars bound for Hangzhou. There were many passengers at the fourth-class ticket booth, and they were purchasing tickets and boarding the cars. Suddenly, there was a gunshot. The passengers were all startled. Upon investigation, it was found that a police officer on duty at the second post of the fourth-class ticket booth (on duty from 6 a.m. to 10 a.m.) was unloading the bullets from his Mauser pistol. Due to a mistake, he had not unloaded all the bullets, and one bullet remained. When the mechanism was pushed, the bullet was ejected from the barrel. Luckily, it did not injure anyone, but all the passengers were startled. The chief of the railway police, Chief Han, personally went to investigate the matter in order to report it for handling.

New Car Purchased by Lin Tingyou, Fellow Villagers Covet and Send a Letter of Extortion 141

Lin Tingyou, a Guangdong native, has been running a rattan shop at No. 186 North Jiangxi Road for many years. Recently, due to the success of his business, he bought a green car a month ago to use as transportation and to solicit sales. His ostentatious behavior was coveted by nearby bandits (Liang Yulin, Feng Guoxing, and Li Dayun, fellow villagers at No. 170 across the street). Liang wrote a threatening letter, demanding 300 yuan and drawing two axes, threatening violence if the money was not paid. The letter was delivered on the seventh of this month. It instructed to put a "Fu" character on the door if the demands were met and to throw a paper-wrapped package of money into a trash can behind the back door of No. 170 the next afternoon. The letter stated that someone would come to collect the money. After receiving the letter, Lin immediately reported it to the Hongkou Police Station. The police station sent Chinese detectives Wang Debiao and Li Zexing in disguise as rickshaw pullers to secretly watch. The victim first put a package of paper that looked like 300 yuan into the trash can and returned. The detectives watched the activity nearby. After a while, Liang and Feng came out of No. 170, lingered around for a long time, looked around, and returned to the house. At 11:30 a.m., Liang Yulin came out again, picked up the paper package, and tried to escape. The detectives rushed forward and arrested him on the spot. Feng and Li were subsequently apprehended in an upstairs room at No. 170 and taken to the police station for detention. The lawyer of the Criminal Court Three of the Special District Court, Zhang Tianyin, detailed the previous events to the court and presented the threatening letter for inspection. He requested a postponement of the investigation to determine if the defendants were involved in other cases. Then, the victim Lin Tingyou testified about the incident. Liang Yulin confessed that he wrote the threatening letter. The case was initiated because he knew that the victim's financial situation was good after he bought a new car. However, the testimonies of the defendants Feng and Li were evasive. Judge Xiao Xiefei instructed that they be remanded into custody for further investigation and interrogation.

Suicide Investigation of Young Woman Yang Guiying 142

Yang Guiying, a 19-year-old woman from Hubei, residing at No. 17 South Chengdu Road, had an argument with her mother the other day for some reason. Afterward, the woman, lost in thought and resentment, became tired of life and secretly swallowed opium paste to commit suicide. Her mother discovered her moaning in bed and sent her to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but to no avail. She soon died. The hospital reported it to the Xinzha Police Station, which dispatched detective Chen Shanji to investigate. The body was taken to the Forensic Inspection Office on Filun Road. Yesterday morning, the Shanghai Special District Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei to visit the office to inspect the body. During the inquest, the mother of the deceased, Yang Yu Shi, 51 years old, testified that her daughter had studied for several years, but she was planning to stop her education. That day, her daughter suddenly asked to continue her studies, but she refused because her daughter was already grown up and had been betrothed to someone in their hometown. This led to an argument, but she did not expect her to take poison. Prosecutor Guo obtained the testimony and, following the instructions, confirmed that the deceased Yang Guiying, female, died from opium poisoning taken before death.

The body was handed over to her mother, Yang Yu Shi, to sign a statement and take it back for burial.

Wo Caizheng Suffers Because of His Concubine 144

Residents of Sijiao Mountain Suffered in the Hurricane 145

Thousands of Houses Were Destroyed, More Than Three Hundred Fishing Boats Were Smashed

Sijiao Mountain, located outside of the Wusong Sanjia Water Inlet and under the jurisdiction of Chongming County, is an isolated island. The residents of the entire island make a living by fishing. During the recent hurricane, the island was directly hit, causing even greater damage. Thousands of houses were destroyed throughout the island, and more than three hundred fishing boats were destroyed and washed away. Seawater flooded the island to a height of about ten feet. Fortunately, most of the fishermen escaped to the top of the mountain and were not drowned, but they have no homes to return to and are waiting to die. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented. The disaster victims have now telegraphed the provincial government and various charitable organizations, appealing for urgent relief to prevent them from starving to death.

They have sent two representatives from the association, Guo Junqing and Ge Xiangyi, to Shanghai to report on the disaster situation and request prompt relief to save the disaster victims from fire and water.

Detailed Report of the Tragic Disaster in Jingyang, Shaanxi 147

The Jisheng Society Hopes for Donations from Philanthropists

The Chinese Jisheng Society recently received a report from the Zhenwu branch of Jingyang County, Shaanxi Province, stating that on the evenings of July 21st and 22nd of this year, there were severe storms with thunder and lightning, and heavy rain poured down. The water depth on the plains was one or two feet. As a result, the Zhiqing Rivers rose violently, and mountain floods occurred suddenly, with the water head being one or two zhang high. When it flowed to Jiaolongbao, the two rivers converged, and the water became even more powerful, inundating countless autumn fields and causing many deaths and injuries. The area surrounding the Luchaoyunyang town Zhangjiatun Yuyu River, covering forty or fifty li, was completely turned into a swamp. The disaster was so severe that it was unbearable to witness. The number of drowned people was countless. There were no districts without disasters. According to the statistics, there were 2,309 households whose names could be verified, 36,198 mu of autumn fields were inundated, 542 houses were collapsed, 146 kilns were flooded, 83 people whose names were confirmed were drowned, one or two dozen livestock were drowned, and seventeen waterwheels were washed away. As for the agricultural implements, tables, stools, and other items of each household, they were also washed away by the water. This year's summer harvest was meager, and the people had no savings. Even the food they had was washed away by the water. They are displaced, starving during the day, and sleeping in the open at night. Moreover, there has been a drought for six years, and no less than thirty or forty thousand people have died of starvation or fled. The survivors have suffered from floods again. The plight of the Jingyang people is truly unprecedented in hundreds of years. Furthermore, from August 7th to 9th, 10th, and 11th, the Jing River rose violently four or five times, inundating more than one hundred hectares of autumn fields along the river. Many guest residents living by the river have already drowned. On the 18th, there was another heavy rain, inundating Yanwang Village, Niaoertan, and other places. All of the autumn fields were submerged. Houses and kilns in the Yuzigou Erlanggou Mushuwan were mostly washed away. The Jinghui Canal bank, which runs from Yanwang Village to Mushuwan, forty or fifty li long and twenty or more li wide, near the northern plateau, was often washed away, submerging even more autumn crops. The autumn fields near the county seat were also inundated by the canal water. This is the third time they have suffered from floods. On the evening of the 23rd, there was a strong wind with thunder and rain. The county stopped soon after, but in Yuyu River under Yunyang and other places, heavy rain poured down, and the water rose on the plains again, inundating the autumn crops and also falling large hailstones, killing birds in the air. This is the fourth time they have suffered from hailstorms. The investigation of the first and second floods in the Qingyu River has been completed. The autumn fields in the plains and plateaus that have not suffered from floods have been severely affected by drought. Most of the grain ears are dry, and the cotton stalks are red and do not produce any fruit. There is no hope for the autumn harvest. The remaining people are in extreme suffering. This is a sad telegram, requesting a large sum of money to save the disaster victims. The society has provided relief to Shaanxi for many years, but the amount is not sufficient. Now, because the income from relief donations is very small, it is hoped that compassionate comrades at home and abroad will have the perseverance and great aspirations to help each other and save lives. The merits and virtues are inconceivable.

Extortion of the Wusong Chamber of Commerce Director 148

The Case Solved on the Spot; Shi Zhigen Confesses Without Reservation

Zhang Yuchi, the director of the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, is a local, seventy years old this year, and runs a soy sauce garden. He is usually quite enthusiastic about local public welfare undertakings. Last year, he fell from a car and injured his foot, and recently relies on people to carry him in and out. The day before yesterday morning, he suddenly received an anonymous letter, which stated, "By order of the Soviet government, a liaison office has been established in Wusong. We are currently in urgent need of funds and are temporarily borrowing 2,000 yuan from your esteemed office," and attached six procedures: (1) The loan amount is fixed at 2,000 yuan and must not be less. (2) Wrap the banknotes in newspaper. (3) Place it in the trash can next to the public toilet north of Wusong Town Railway Station at 8:00 PM on September 9th. (4) Do not discuss this loan with outsiders before the loan procedures are cleared. (5) Do not report to the police, and do not send anyone to secretly investigate that night, or you will be dealt with by a handgun. (6) If you do not comply with the above conditions, your house will be reduced to ashes," etc. After receiving the letter, Zhang reported it to the Seventh District Public Security Bureau. After receiving the report, District Chief Gong Xikui, after discussing a plan with District Officer Yin Gongtian, led detectives and secretly went to ambush in a hidden place at around 8:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 9th). They first placed a package wrapped in paper in the designated trash can, and attached two bells below the package. Around 9:00 PM, several people came and lingered near the trash can. Then, one person first used a flashlight to shine into the trash can, and seeing the paper package inside, reached out to pick it up, triggering the attached bells. The ambushing detectives immediately rushed forward and captured four people on the spot. They were all taken to the district. After interrogation by District Chief Gong, one was Shi Zhigen, one was Zhu Ziwen, one was Chen Xiaomao, and one was Tao Hegen. Shi Zhigen confessed that due to financial difficulties, he wrote the letter for extortion without reservation. The remaining Zhu Ziwen was found to have no suspicion of collusion and was released on bail pending trial. Chen Xiaomao and Tao Hegen were released without charge. Shi Zhigen was detained and taken to the bureau yesterday afternoon for interrogation.

Female Servant Hangs Herself After Losing Job 149

Lodging in Someone's Home Causes No Small Amount of Trouble

A woman named Wang Guo, from Haizhou, is currently forty years old and worked as a maid in the home of someone surnamed in the Ximen Road area of the French Concession. Recently, due to frequent thefts in the employer's home, she was blamed for negligence and was dismissed. Ms. Wang went to the home of a fellow maid, Ms. Yang Han, who was from Anhui, requesting lodging and planning to find another employer. Ms. Yang Han, because she was still working as a maid at her employer's home, could not accommodate outsiders, and led Ms. Wang to the home of her younger sister, Ms. Yang Zhu, at No. 34 Taihe Lane, Boer Road, for temporary lodging. Unexpectedly, Ms. Wang suddenly attempted suicide. On the afternoon of the 9th, while Ms. Yang Zhu was out, she used a cloth strip to hang herself. When Ms. Yang Zhu, the younger sister of Ms. Yang Han, returned home at 6:00 PM, she discovered that Ms. Wang had already died. The second landlord, Liu Abao, reported it to the French Concession Police, who sent detectives to investigate. The body was then taken by vehicle to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for examination. There were no family members in Shanghai. Yesterday, a report was made to the Second Special District Court, which appointed Prosecutor Wang Ren to come to the site. After examining the body, it was determined that the deceased, Wang Guo, had indeed died by hanging herself. Witnesses Yang Han, Yang Zhu, and the second landlord Liu Abao were questioned about the circumstances of the discovery. It was then ordered that the body be handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall for photographs and burial, pending identification by relatives.

Yan Mingqing Accused of Embezzling Funds 150

Yan Yuanqing, 35 years old, from Haimen, Zhejiang Province, worked as a traveling salesman for the Bise Canning Food Company on Lagna Road in the French Concession. Recently, manager Chen Zusi discovered that Yan had been secretly collecting account payments from various local and out-of-town shops from August 1st to the end of the month, totaling 311 yuan from several households in Shanghai, including Daoxiangcun, Tongfuzhai, Caizhizhai, and Yuexiangzhai. The amount of money he had collected from out-of-town shops also totalled to hundreds of yuan. When Yan was asked about this, he was evasive, so the police were notified. Detective Wang Maonan arrested Yan and brought him to the Second Special District Court, charging him with embezzlement. The prosecution stated that the accounts collected by the defendant from out-of-town shops had not yet been verified, and requested that the verified local accounts be used as evidence. The defendant claimed that he was buying goods on behalf of the plaintiff and that he normally took a 5% discount, resulting in nearly 20,000 yuan in business transactions. According to his calculations, the plaintiff should have returned money to him and that he had no use for the false accusations. The court ordered a postponement until the 19th and instructed the plaintiff to present the account books and evidence for further examination. The defendant was released on a 500-yuan security bond, and without a guarantor, he was detained.

Ge Jingkang Robbed Immediately Upon Arrival in Shanghai 151

Ge Jingkang, from Jiaxing, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday morning on the Xin Jiangtian steamboat from Ningbo. After arriving in Shanghai, he hired a rickshaw to go to a friend's place on Beijing Road. Unexpectedly, when he reached the Huangpu Bund intersection on Zhoushan Road in the French Concession, five robbers suddenly blocked his way and robbed him of 25 yuan before fleeing. Detective Wang Baoming and patrol officers, hearing the alarm, arrived in time and arrested one of the robbers, Chen Guofang, and took him to the police station. At 11:00 AM that morning, he was sent to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer first stated that the case still required the arrest of accomplices and requested a postponement for further interrogation. Judge Wang briefly questioned the defendant and ordered him to be detained and the case postponed for further interrogation.

Illegal Sale of Red Pills Leads to Conviction 152

Wang Zonghan, from Suzhou, along with Chen Aibao, Tang Chunyuan, Xue Songbai, and others, were engaged in the illegal sale of red pills. They were caught the day before yesterday in Room 17 of the Haitongchun Inn in Yude Lane, Yunnan Road, by Detective Li Shugui, who found 13 taels of red pills. They were taken to the Laoza Gate Police Station and subsequently sent to the First Special District District Court. Judge Feng Shide, after examining the evidence, found them guilty and sentenced Wang Zonghan to one year and six months in prison, and Chen and the other three to eight months each. The red pills were confiscated.

Joint Executive Committee of Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industries Association 153

The Joint Association of Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Trade Associations held a temporary executive meeting at 5:00 PM on September 9th. The matters discussed are recorded below. Chairman Zhang Dalian reported on the purpose of the meeting. (1) The Qidong County Alcohol Industry Association sent a letter requesting the transfer to the Taxation Department, requesting a reduction in the tax rate on white liquor to alleviate the difficulties of businesses. It was resolved to forward the letter to the Taxation Department with the request. (2) Due to the complexity of the association's affairs, it was agreed to add two standing committee members. Yao Jiansan received seven votes or more. The election of two people as standing committee members should be reported to the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Department for record. (3) The Chairman of the Tobacco Association, Chen Liangyu, sent a letter of resignation. The resolution was approved. As the position of Chairman should not be vacant for long, the issue of how to handle it was discussed. The vote resulted in Mr. Yu Xunlu winning eight votes and being elected as the Standing Chairman of the Tobacco Association. This should be reported to the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Department for record. (4) The general meeting handed over a case of members who had not been approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and had no supporting documents to the meeting. The resolution was to temporarily order them to withdraw from the association. It was immediately sent to all members who had not reported for record, requiring them to send supporting documents to the association before the 20th of this month. If there is no proof at the end of the period, according to the resolution of the General Assembly, they will be temporarily ordered to withdraw from the association. After the filing procedures are corrected, they will still join the association as members. When the deadline expires, the roster will be corrected, and a document will be submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for submission to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval and record, in order to comply with laws and regulations and complete the procedures. Passed.

Attention to Ships Sailing to Tanggu 155

Seamark Notice (No. 1045) from the Marine Department of the Inspectorate General of Customs states: "For the purpose of announcement, the Inspector General of Customs opened a case. In accordance with the agreement of the 1930 Lisbon Conference on Unified Maritime Buoys and Lighthouses, all regulations of the Tianjin Customs regarding the display of tidal rise and fall and water level height signals, as listed in the attached diagram, should be implemented simultaneously at the flag-raising point in Tanggu and the Dagukou River Blocking Sand Lightship from the daytime of October 1st of this year. At the same time, the current signaling methods will be abolished. All matters related to the regulations of various signals should be listed separately and issued separately, instructing the Inspector and Engineers to comply with the regulations, etc." The attached list is hereby announced, and all the items listed in the order are recorded below for the information of Chinese and foreign shipping merchants. (1) The flag-raising point in Tanggu should display various day and night signals. (2) The Dagukou River Blocking Sand Lightship should only display daytime signals. (3) Water level height: The water level height shown by the flag-raising point in Tanggu and the Dagukou River Blocking Sand Lightship is the depth of the River Blocking Sand Channel, and is calculated in feet. (4) Related charts: Maritime Chart No. 1025 of the Ministry of the Navy of the Republic of China, August 31, 22nd year of the Republic of China, Marine Department Inspector and Engineer Li Manxi.

Exit Road to Pudong at Xidu Pier Blocked 157

The Xidu Pier in Yangjing, Pudong, is one of the public ferry piers in Pudong. It was previously submitted by the Pond Engineering Relief Bureau to the Shanghai County Magistrate, who reported it in detail to the Shanghai Daoyin and the Jiangsu Diplomatic Commissioner, who approved it, stating that if there were requests to raise and fill mud, a road should be left out, etc. Now, the Shanghai Municipal Public Utility Bureau, in order to develop the municipal ferry, has changed the location of the Xidu Pier and blocked the old Xidu Pier's exit road to Pudong, causing opposition from local residents. If the Municipal Ferry route is to go from the Tongren Pier in Shanghai to Gaoqiao in the east, according to the plan of the Public Utility Bureau, the people of Yangjing who travel between Pudong and Puxi must take the Municipal Ferry and detour to the Tongren Pier in Shanghai. However, the old Xidu Pier and the newly located pier both have two exit roads to Pudong that can be used for crossing. Now that the location has been changed and one road has been blocked, the residents are suffering from inconvenience.

Calligraphy and Painting News 158

Exhibition by Wu Jiang's Veteran Painter Yuan Tao'an in Wu Jiang

Veteran painter Yuan Tao'an has loved calligraphy and painting since childhood. He studied the six principles of painting with Hu Gongchou of Huating for more than forty years and has deeply grasped the essence of the ancients. His landscapes are rich in atmosphere and stand out from the ordinary. In the past, when he traveled as an official to the old capital, people sought his work one after another. In recent years, he has secluded himself from politics and supported himself by selling art in Ping. This spring, due to the troubles in Pingjin, he returned south and settled in Wumen. Recently, in response to the invitation of friends here, he came to Shanghai a few days ago, bringing with him more than a hundred pieces of his latest works and family collection of authentic works, which are scheduled to open for exhibition at the Guowen Communications Agency downstairs in the Continental Commercial Building on Er Ma Road starting from September 12th. The prices are reasonable.

Weather Report 161

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The sky is cloudy. Cyclones around Taiwan and the northern part of the China Sea are intensifying, and the weather is deteriorating. This is because a small hurricane has formed southeast of the Dongsha Islands, or it may proceed to the northwest-west. Its center was within 120 miles of the intersection of 20 degrees north latitude and 119 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. The hurricane north of Yap Island appears to be moving northwest. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 90.7 and the lowest was 70.5. On the same day last year, the highest was 88.3 and the lowest was 67.6.

Education News

Important News 162

Miss Hu Lai, Principal of Somerville College, Oxford, to Visit China for Investigation

And Plans to Lecture at Various Universities

(Nanjing, 10th) The China Committee of the Universities of London has sent Miss Hu Lai, the former Principal of Somerville College, Oxford University, to China. She will spend three months investigating the recent educational situation in China, with a special focus on women's education. She plans to lecture at various Chinese universities on the following topics: (1) The organization and purpose of British education; (2) British public opinion and government; (3) British girls' sports; (4) The life of female students in British universities. Miss Hu Lai has already left England, representing Britain at the Pan-Pacific Academic Conference. She has now arrived in the United States and will soon depart for China.

Ministry of Education Orders Investigation of Provincial Middle Schools 163

The Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating that the twenty-first year has long since ended. The statistics for the middle schools in each province and city for the twenty-first year are urgently needed for investigation and compilation. Therefore, detailed statistical forms for middle schools for the twenty-first year have been drafted, along with instructions for filling them out. These are hereby issued, and you are to fill them out and report them within three months of receiving this order, without delay or omission, which is of utmost importance. Furthermore, the statistical forms for middle schools for the twenty-first year are divided into two types: individual school forms and provincial/municipal summary forms. The former should be forwarded by the provincial department to each school to be filled out and reported, while the latter should be compiled in detail by the provincial department/bureau. Both should be filled out completely, along with the individual school forms, and reported to the Ministry by the end of November of this year.

Ministry of Education Orders Investigation of Education for the Blind and Deaf 164

The Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating that it is urgently necessary to separately investigate the overall situation of education for the blind and deaf nationwide. Therefore, a questionnaire on the overall situation of education for the blind and deaf in each province and city, as well as a survey form on the overall situation of education for the blind and deaf, are hereby issued. You are to investigate the overall situation of public and private education for the blind and deaf within your jurisdiction within one month of receiving this document, and fill out and return the questionnaire and the items listed on the form separately. These schools are not yet universally established and are few in number, making the investigation easy. The provincial department must fill out and report on time for evaluation. If the "province" or "city" still does not have such schools, the situation of not having organized them should also be reported at any time, which is of utmost importance. This is the order.

Standing Committee of the Educational Film Association 165

The Standing Committee of the Chinese Educational Film Association held its third meeting at the Ministry of Education on the afternoon of the 9th, from 3:00 PM to 7:00 PM. Present were Standing Committee members Chen Lifu, Guo Cunshou, Wu Yan Yin, Peng Baichuan, Chu Minyi (represented by Dai Ce, Deputy Director of the Design Group of the Association), Wang Pingling, Deputy Director of the Editorial Group of the Association, and Li Jiaxiang, Standing Committee member of the Film Censorship Committee (invited to attend). Guo You Shou chaired the meeting, and Wang Zhan recorded the proceedings. The following matters were discussed: (1) Review of the organizational charter of the Shanghai Branch; passed. (2) Review of the work plan of the Shanghai Branch; passed. (3) The Shandong Provincial Public Education Center reported difficulties in selecting and renting educational films for its affiliated public cinema and requested assistance. It was decided that the Shanghai Branch should negotiate the film rental methods. (4) Compilation of the Chinese Film Yearbook; passed. It was decided that it would be jointly organized by this association and the Film Censorship Committee, and a joint committee would be formed (details attached below). (5) The Shanghai Branch requested that the Central Propaganda Committee be asked to send films produced by the association to Shanghai for screening to promote propaganda. It was decided to recommend Peng Baichuan to contact the Central Propaganda Committee to handle the matter. (6) Review of new membership applications; forty new members were approved (other cases temporarily raised or reported by committee members were discussed briefly). The approved procedures for compiling the Chinese Film Yearbook are recorded below: (1) The Chinese Film Yearbook will be compiled by a compilation committee consisting of five members appointed by the Chinese Educational Film Association and the Film Censorship Committee (the Chinese Educational Film Association has already nominated Wang Pingling and Dai Ce, and the Shanghai Branch has nominated Pan Gongzhan; the remaining two members will be nominated by the Film Censorship Committee). (2) The compilation committee will have a chairman, elected by the committee members, who will oversee the compilation. (3) The working period for the compilation committee is tentatively set at three and a half months, from September 15th to December 31st. (4) The outline for the yearbook will be drafted by the compilation committee and submitted to the two associations for approval. (5) The compilation committee members should be appropriately compensated by the two associations. (6) The funding methods required (omitted).

One of the Shen Bao Series 167

Publication of Military Preparations in the United States, Japan, and the Soviet Union

The world situation is becoming increasingly dangerous, and the eve of World War II is upon us. The situation in the Pacific is urgent, and our country is being forced to face a critical moment of survival. In this dangerous situation, it is imperative to quickly understand the current state of military preparedness of the United States, Japan, and the Soviet Union, the prominent players in this situation. The book "Military Preparations in the United States, Japan, and the Soviet Union" by Mr. Yang Bokai meets this need with a detailed explanation. The entire book has three chapters, providing an exhaustive explanation of the history, development, current status, organization, and strength of the land, sea, and air forces, as well as new types of military preparations, of the three countries. It includes various tables for comparison, making it an invaluable resource. All Chinese people and those interested in research should prepare a copy. The actual price is thirty cents. It is published by the special distribution department of this newspaper. A special price is offered for one month during the autumn school opening season. A 30% discount is offered for purchases of ten or more copies.

British Man Takes Home the All-American Tennis Singles Championship 174

Hughills Loses, America Despairs | The Champion Will Be Either Perry or Crawford |

(Forest Hills, 9th, Reuters) The All-American Tennis Singles Championship will be won by a British man. The contestants competing for the title in the final are Crawford, the Wimbledon and Australian champion, and Perry, the leader of the British Davis Cup team.

Perry Takes a Sharp Turn | Under the gaze of 8,000 spectators today, Perry defeated Stoffen in the quarter-finals in three straight sets, 6-3 in the first set and 6-2 in the second and third sets. Stoffen has never suffered such a crushing defeat since participating in first-class tennis. Perry's forehand and backhand shots were sharp, and his opponent struggled to cope, resulting in this outcome.

Crawford Ends American Hope | Crawford defeated Hughills in three straight sets, 7-5, 6-4, 6-3. Hughills, who was the only remaining American player, was disappointed and defeated. Crawford remained calm, and his backhand returns were accurate and mechanical, resulting in many points. Hughills was quick and agile, but had too many out-of-bounds balls.

Yang Yuanhua Creates Two New National Records 175

100-meter Backstroke in 1 Minute 29.4 Seconds | 200-meter Breaststroke in 3 Minutes 19.6 Seconds | City Games Swimming Competition Concludes

Swimmer Yang Yuanhua created two new national records yesterday in the 100-meter backstroke and 200-meter breaststroke, adding much color to this year's Shanghai City Games swimming competition. His time in the 100-meter backstroke was 1 minute 29.4 seconds, and in the 200-meter breaststroke, it was 3 minutes 19.6 seconds, an improvement over the new record he set in the preliminary round on the first day, which is especially commendable. The audience at the Jiaotong University swimming pool was even more enthusiastic. All the swimming events in the City Games concluded yesterday. The details are recorded below.

50-Meter Freestyle 176

The first final event was the men's 50-meter freestyle. Wen Jingling's victory was as expected by the reporter, without a doubt, but the competition was fierce, with splashing waves, making it very exciting. Yu Rongbang was defeated by Yu Heng, and the famous Yin Yanjun fell to fourth place. Wen's time was 30.2 seconds. The women's 50-meter final was also very even, with only four people competing. Gong Xiji, the "fat lady," entered the water later and finally won the championship, but the performance was not very exciting.

City Games Swimming Competition, from right to left: Breaststroke Champion Ms. Hu Qiyuan, 100-meter Champion Ms. Zheng Baoxuan, 400-meter and 1500-meter Champion Zhou Dayun, 40-meter Champion Wen Jingling.

(Photo by Ye Lie of this newspaper)

Backstroke Breaks National Record

Yang Yuanhua 1 Minute 29.4 Seconds | In the second final, the 100-meter backstroke, Yang Yuanhua, who set a new national record of 1 minute 32.4 seconds in the preliminary round the day before, further shortened his time to 1 minute 29.4 seconds, breaking the national record again (the old record was 1 minute 38 seconds by Zeng Rongzhong), which is very gratifying. Yang exchanged splashes with one hand, as if in rhythm, with a consistent speed, advancing calmly, demonstrating a deep level of skill. Only two people competed in the women's backstroke, one was the "big guy" Gong Xiji, and the other was the "little girl" Bao Lengxue, one big and one small, contrasting interestingly. When the "big guy" Gong entered the water, because of her heavy body and improper technique, the water splashed and splashed on the spectators by the pool, causing them a lot of trouble. As a result, the bigger one won, and the smaller one lost.

1500 Meters

In the 1500-meter freestyle final, it was necessary to go back and forth 30 times (i.e., 60 one-way trips). The 400-meter champion, Zhou Dayun, was rich in stamina, his body rippling with the water, leaping forward. At one meter of the course, he had already exceeded the second person by two pools, while Zheng Guanxian retired from the water due to exhaustion after sixteen round trips. Zhou remained consistent throughout, brave and persistent. In the end, Zhou beat the second, Chen Yuquan, by 100 meters, with a time of 26 minutes 55.4 seconds.

Breaststroke Also Breaks National Record 177

Yang Yuanhua 3 Minutes 19.6 Seconds | Next was the 200-meter breaststroke, with the women's race first. The "little girl" Hu Qiyuan floated on the water, her posture was beautiful, back and forth a total of eight times, from beginning to end, without the slightest slack, she won the championship with 4 minutes 27 seconds, earning the audience's warm applause. The second, Gong Xiji, was one pool behind, the third, Zhang Jiazhen, the fourth, Tan Ruoju, two pools away from the third, still continued to implement the original intention, completed the whole process, the spirit is commendable.

In the men's group, Li Rixin, who set a new national record of 3 minutes 27.2 seconds in the preliminary round the day before, was defeated by Yang Yuanhua in the final, and Yang also broke the national record, and the time was 3 minutes 19.6 seconds, further breaking Li's new record. Li was runner-up, and the time seemed to be an improvement over his preliminary round (the old record was 3 minutes 27.8 seconds by Ma Zhihui). The competition between Yang and Li was fierce, and the whole pool suddenly became tense, and Li finally lagged behind by three or four yards.

100-Meter Freestyle

Men Have Fierce Battle, Women Very Funny

The men's 100-meter freestyle final was one of the most exciting scenes. Yin Yanjun, mindful of the lag in the 50 meters, strove to go upstream, fiercely competing with Zhou Rui, the others also did not relax, stirring up waves, the momentum was magnificent. Zhou won the championship, Yin was the runner-up, the difference was three yards away, the time was 1 minute 13.1 seconds. The start of the women's group was quite funny. The first time Hu Qiying was eager to try, and fell into the water before the order was given. At the same time, Hu Qiyuan involuntarily followed into the water. Rising out of the water to swim again, the two were as timid as mice. After the order was given, Qi Ying was still stunned and did not enter the water. Seeing others going forward, she jumped into the water. Yuan, seeing Qi Ying not entering the water, stood in the water again. Seeing Qi Ying entering the water, she started to swim again, and had already been overtaken by Gong Xiji by three or four meters. This was due to lack of experience. As a result, Gong was the first, and Ms. Yuan changed to swimming breaststroke in the middle, and finished third.

Public Doubles Semi-Quarterfinals: Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang Eliminated 182

Lost 1-3 to Liang Deguang and Carlsen | Our Rotary Cup Doubles Representatives Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang lost 1-3 to the Sino-American partnership of Liang Deguang and Carlsen at the Chinese Tennis Courts at 4:00 PM yesterday. This was a scene from the semi-quarterfinals of the Public Doubles of the Grass Tennis Association. The two sides had once clashed, but it did not end due to the lateness of the day. With the consent of both parties, it was decided to replay it yesterday to fight for the right to the quarterfinals. Since Liang Deguang and Carlsen won, they will meet Stoke and Koehl in the quarterfinals. First Set When the battle began, Zheng and Yu were arm-in-arm, with a wonderful cooperation, so their progress was very rapid. If they could maintain their sharpness throughout, they could have finished the first set in the局 after 5-2, but due to slackness, they won 6-4.

Second Set At the beginning, Zheng and Yu were still very strong, but after 3-3, they suddenly encountered the opponent's correct chop and fierce pressure, turning into a bad situation, and finally lost the second set 4-6.

Third Set It is inevitable to disappoint that Zheng and Yu could have won but failed. At that time, they were leading 5-4, but suddenly suffered a blow with a decadent spirit, losing three consecutive games, and instead lost 7-5. The spectators on the wall all regretted it.

Fourth Set At this time, Liang Deguang and Carlsen were stern and kept the net, with no opportunity to attack. Liang Deguang's baseline was just right, and Carlsen's serve was fast and powerful. Although Zheng and Yu tried their best to resist everything, they still fell at a disadvantage. Liang and Carlsen then completed the set with 6-2. Liang Deguang 4|6 Zheng Zhaojia

(1) All accommodation matters for the Games will be handled by the Accommodation Department of the Accommodation Group. (2) Regarding welcoming and sending off referees and athletes, the Accommodation Group has agreed on the following cooperative arrangements with the China Travel Service: 1. Before departing, all sports units or referees should obtain baggage stickers or tags from the local China Travel Service, clearly marking the name of the group, the individual's name, and the destination for identification. 2. Matters such as exchanging tickets for free or discounted tickets for train and ship berths, as well as checking baggage, should be coordinated with the local China Travel Service. When departing, the number of people, the train schedule, the ship name, and the arrival date should be telegraphed to the Accommodation Group through the China Travel Service. 3. All matters concerning liaison between the various units and the Accommodation Group should be handled by the team leader for the sake of standardization. 4. Large baggage of referees and athletes may be handed over to the Accommodation Group staff for safekeeping, but small personal items (such as handbags, small wicker baskets, etc.) should be carried by the individuals themselves. 5. Upon arrival of each group, the team leader shall hand over the large baggage to the Accommodation Group staff for transportation to the dormitory, and then hand it over to the team leader for receipt. The same procedure shall be followed upon departure, with the Accommodation Group responsible for transporting the baggage to the station or pier and handing it over to the respective team leaders. However, the team leader shall be responsible for observing the checking, collection, and delivery of baggage consigned to the railway to avoid errors. 6. After the team leader hands over the baggage to the Accommodation Group, no one may arbitrarily remove items before the baggage has been transported to its destination and properly delivered. 7. After the team leader hands over the baggage to the Accommodation Group staff, the Accommodation Group will issue a receipt, affix a label to each item of baggage, and transport it to its destination. The Accommodation Group's responsibility ends when the team leader receives the baggage without error and returns the receipt. If athletes are careless on the train and errors or losses occur, the Accommodation Department will do its best to assist in correction or investigation, but will not be liable for other responsibilities. 8. The Accommodation Group will have staff stationed at the Xiaguan Railway Station, Pukou Railway Station, Jiangbian Wharf, and the Games venue, together with China Travel Service staff, to handle the reception, collection, and care of baggage. 9. (Attached is a list of China Travel Service branches in various commercial ports throughout the country: Beiping, Hangzhou, Xuzhou, Tianjin, Hong Kong, Qingdao, Jinan, Zhenjiang, Hankou, Jiujiang, Zhengzhou, Changsha, Tongguan, Yichang. Sports teams and referees who are departing from places without a China Travel Service can contact a branch of the China Travel Service in the above-mentioned locations along the way.) (3) Anyone wishing to host a banquet for referees and athletes must register with the Accommodation Department three days in advance so that a schedule can be arranged. Except in special circumstances, requests for rescheduling will not be granted. (4) In order to facilitate the check-in procedures and inquiries for referees and athletes, the Accommodation Group has set up information desks at the Games venue, Xiaguan Railway Station, Pukou Railway Station, Xiaguan Jiangbian, and the Lizhi Society. (5) Referees must first present their letter of appointment from the Games upon arrival, collect a registration form, fill it out in detail, exchange it for a Games handbook and badge, and a lodging permit, and then move into the dormitory in sequence according to the number on the permit. (6) Upon arrival, each team's athletes should first have their team leader report to the check-in desk, submit verification documents, collect a registration form from the information desk, fill it out in detail, exchange it for a Games handbook, badge, and lodging permit, and then move into the dormitory in sequence according to the number on the permit.
